|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-607">collation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-607">collation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-608">一組決定如何比較、排序和呈現資料的規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-608">A set of rules that determines how data is compared, ordered, and presented.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-609">collection</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-609">collection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-610">包含了一組相關物件的物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-610">An object that contains a set of related objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-611">每當集合中發生變更時，物件在集合中的位置都會變更；因此，集合中任何特定物件的位置可能會不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-611">An object's position in the collection can change whenever a change occurs in the collection; therefore, the position of any specific object in a collection may vary.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-612">收集項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-612">collection item</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-613">收集器類型的執行個體，它是使用一組特定的輸入屬性和收集頻率所建立，而且會用於收集特定類型的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-613">An instance of a collector type that is created with a specific set of input properties and collection frequency, and that is used to gather specific types of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-614">收集模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-614">collection mode</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-615">收集資料並將其上傳到管理資料倉儲的頻率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-615">The frequency at which data is collected and uploaded to the management data warehouse.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-616">收集組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-616">collection set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-617">使用者可以透過使用者介面與其互動的一組收集項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-617">A group of collection items with which a user can interact through the user interface.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-618">收集器類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-618">collector type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-619">包裝 SQL Server Integration Services 封裝的邏輯包裝函式，可提供實際機制來收集資料，並將資料上傳到管理資料倉儲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-619">A logical wrapper around the SQL Server Integration Services packages that provide the actual mechanism for collecting data and uploading it to the management data warehouse.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-620">共置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-620">collocate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-621">選取資料分割資料表，其中包含要在此分割資料行上與這個資料表聯結的相關資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-621">To select a partitioned table that contains related data and join with this table on the partitioning column.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-622">共現性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-622">collocation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-623">資料分割資料表和索引根據對等資料分割函數進行資料分割的狀況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-623">A condition whereby partitioned tables and indexes are partitioned according to equivalent partition functions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-624">色彩範圍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-624">color range</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-625">可供顯示裝置使用的色彩範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-625">The range of colors available to a display device.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-626">色彩規則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-626">color rule</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-627">套用的一種規則，可為多邊形、線條，以及代表點或多邊形中心點的標記填滿色彩。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-627">A rule that applies to fill colors for polygons, lines, and markers that represent points or polygon center points.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-628">色階 (color scale)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-628">color scale</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-629">僅顯示色彩規則結果的色階。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-629">A scale that displays the results of color rules only.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-630">column</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-630">column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-631">資料庫資料表的每一個資料列中的區域，可儲存資料表所呈現之物件的一些屬性的資料值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-631">The area in each row of a database table that stores the data value for some attribute of the object modeled by the table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-632">資料行繫結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-632">column binding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-633">在資料來源檢視中，Analysis Services 物件與資料行的繫結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-633">The binding of an Analysis Services object to a column in a data source view.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-634">資料行分隔符號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-634">column delimiter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-635">在匯入/匯出的 CSV 檔案中，用於彼此分隔資料行的字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-635">A character which separates columns from each other in the CSV file being imported/exported.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-636">資料行篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-636">column filter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-637">用於限制快照式、交易式或合併式發行集中所要包含之資料行的篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-637">A filter that restricts columns that are to be included as part of a snapshot, transactional, or merge publication.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-638">資料行模式設定檔</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-638">Column Pattern Profile</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-639">包含一組規則運算式的報表，其中涵蓋了字串資料行中值的指定百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-639">A report containing a set of regular expressions that cover the specified percentage of values in a string column.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-640">資料行集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-640">column set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-641">不具類型的 XML 表示，可將資料表的所有疏鬆資料行結合到結構化輸出中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-641">An untyped XML representation that combines all the sparse columns of a table into a structured output.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-642">資料行層級定序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-642">column-level collation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-643">支援單一執行個體中的多重定序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-643">Supporting multiple collations in a single instance.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-644">資料行層級條件約束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-644">column-level constraint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-645">在建立或變更資料表時，資料行定義內所指定的條件約束定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-645">A constraint definition that is specified within a column definition when a table is created or altered.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-646">資料行格線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-646">Columns Grid</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-647">資料表設計工具中可編輯的格線結構，此結構會列出資料表的資料行，以及關於每個資料行的其他資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-647">An editable grid structure in the Table Designer that lists the columns of a table and additional information about each column.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-648">資料行存放區索引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-648">columnstore index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-649">將每一個資料行儲存在個別磁碟頁集合中，而不是每個頁面儲存多個資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-649">Stores each column in a separate set of disk pages rather than storing multiple rows per page.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-650">COM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-650">COM</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-651">以物件為基礎的程式設計模型，專門設計來提升軟體互通性。它可以讓兩個或多個應用程式或元件輕易地彼此合作，即使它們是由不同的供應商、在不同的時間、以不同的程式語言所撰寫或者在執行不同作業系統的不同電腦上執行也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-651">An object-based programming model designed to promote software interoperability; it allows two or more applications or components to easily cooperate with one another, even if they were written by different vendors, at different times, in different programming languages, or if they are running on different computers running different operating systems.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-652">命令緩衝區</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-652">command buffer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-653">用來保留使用者所輸入之命令的記憶體區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-653">An area in memory in which commands entered by the user are kept.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-654">命令緩衝區可讓使用者重複命令，而不用完全重新輸入命令，也可讓使用者編輯過去的命令來變更某個引數或更正錯誤、恢復命令，或是取得過去命令的清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-654">A command buffer can enable the user to repeat commands without retyping them completely, edit past commands to change some argument or correct a mistake, undo commands, or obtain a list of past commands.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-655">命令提示字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-655">command prompt</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-656">作業系統與使用者之間的介面，使用者可在其中輸入命令語言文字字串來傳遞給命令解譯器執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-656">An interface between the operating system and the user in which the user types command language strings of text that are passed to the command interpreter for execution.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-657">命令關聯性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-657">command relationship</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-658">提供以自然語言問題或命令為基礎的硬體指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-658">Provides instructions to hardware based on natural-language questions or commands.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-659">認可</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-659">commit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-660">將交易開始之後的所有資料庫、Cube 或維度變更儲存起來的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-660">An operation that saves all changes to databases, cubes, or dimensions made since the start of a transaction.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-661">認可預覽</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-661">Commit Preview</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-662">視窗的標題，此標題會顯示認可作業期間要採取的動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-662">The title of a window that displays actions to be taken during the commit operation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-663">認可</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-663">committed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-664">已記錄而且無法回復的交易特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-664">Characteristic of a transaction that is logged and cannot be rolled back.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-665">商品通路索引公式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-665">commodity channel index formula</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-666">計算商品每日平均價格與移動平均值之間平均標準差的公式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-666">A formula that calculates the mean deviation of the daily average price of a commodity from the moving average.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-667">高於 100 的值表示商品過度採購，低於 -100 的值表示商品過度銷售。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-667">A value above 100 indicates that the commodity is overbought, and a value below -100 indicates that the commodity is oversold.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-668">比較子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-668">comparator</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-669">比較兩個項目來判斷是否相同的裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-669">A device for comparing two items to determine whether they are equal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-670">例如在電子產品中，比較子是指比較兩個輸入電壓並指出哪一個較高的電路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-670">In electronics, for example, a comparator is a circuit that compares two input voltages and indicates which is higher.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-671">編譯錯誤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-671">compilation error</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-672">編譯應用程式時所發生的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-672">An error which occurs while compiling an application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-673">這些編譯錯誤通常是因為語法輸入錯誤而發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-673">These compilation errors typically occur because syntax was entered incorrectly.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-674">編譯時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-674">compile time</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-675">執行程式編譯所需的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-675">The amount of time required to perform a compilation of a program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-676">編譯時間的範圍從幾分之一秒到幾個小時，取決於程式的大小和複雜度、編譯器的速度以及硬體的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-676">Compile time can range from a fraction of a second to many hours, depending on the size and complexity of the program, the speed of the compiler, and the performance of the hardware.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-677">完整資料庫還原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-677">complete database restore</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-678">完整資料庫備份、最新差異資料庫備份 (如果有的話)，以及在完整資料庫備份之後所建立之記錄備份 (如果有的話) 的還原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-678">A restore of a full database backup, the most recent differential database backup (if any), and the log backups (if any) taken since the full database backup.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-679">複雜事件處理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-679">complex event processing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-680">在幾乎零延遲的情況下，根據宣告式查詢和模式規格，以連續和累加的方式處理多個來源的事件資料流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-680">The continuous and incremental processing of event streams from multiple sources based on declarative query and pattern specifications with near-zero latency.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-681">元件物件模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-681">Component Object Model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-682">以物件為基礎的程式設計模型，專門設計來提升軟體互通性。它可以讓兩個或多個應用程式或元件輕易地彼此合作，即使它們是由不同的供應商、在不同的時間、以不同的程式語言所撰寫或者在執行不同作業系統的不同電腦上執行也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-682">An object-based programming model designed to promote software interoperability; it allows two or more applications or components to easily cooperate with one another, even if they were written by different vendors, at different times, in different programming languages, or if they are running on different computers running different operating systems.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-683">可組合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-683">composable</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-684">與組成複雜查詢的能力有關，方法是使用查詢元件 (物件或運算子) 當做可重複使用的建置組塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-684">Pertaining to the ability to form complex queries by using query components (objects or operators) as reusable building blocks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-685">這項作業是將查詢元件連結在一起，或將查詢元件彼此封裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-685">This is done by linking query components together or encapsulating query components within each other.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-686">撰寫環境</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-686">composed environment</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-687">從虛擬機器建立而來的虛擬環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-687">A virtual environment that was created from virtual machines.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-688">這些虛擬機器是在 Microsoft 測試管理員之外建立，而且已經在主機群組上部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-688">Those virtual machines were created outside of Microsoft Test Manager and are already deployed on a host group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-689">複合式索引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-689">composite index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-690">利用資料表的多個資料行來建立資料索引的索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-690">An index that uses more than one column in a table to index data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-691">複合索引鍵</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-691">composite key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-692">由檔案中的兩個或多個欄位、資料表中的資料行、或關聯中的屬性組成定義的索引鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-692">A key whose definition consists of two or more fields in a file, columns in a table, or attributes in a relation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-693">撰寫階層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-693">compositional hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-694">概念屬於階層之一部分的一組實體，例如父實體和子實體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-694">A set of entities that are conceptually part of a hierarchy, such as a parent entity and a child entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-695">資料作業要求實體必須當做一個單位來處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-695">Data operations require that the entities be treated as a single unit.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-696">計算資料行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-696">computed column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-697">資料表中，將在執行階段計算其值的虛擬資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-697">A virtual column in a table whose value is computed at run time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-698">計算欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-698">computed field</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-699">在已格式化的通知中利用 Transact-SQL 運算式所計算的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-699">A value in a formatted notification that has been computed by using a Transact-SQL expression.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-700">COM 結構化儲存體檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-700">COM-structured storage file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-701">Data Transformation Services (DTS) 所使用的元件物件模型 (COM) 複合檔案，可儲存已儲存之 DTS 封裝的版本歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-701">A component object model (COM) compound file used by Data Transformation Services (DTS) to store the version history of a saved DTS package.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-702">串連 (concatenation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-702">concatenation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-703">將兩個或多個字元字串或運算式結合成單一字元字串或運算式，或將兩個或多個二進位字串或運算式結合成單一二進位字串或運算式的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-703">The process of combining two or more character strings or expressions into a single character string or expression, or combining two or more binary strings or expressions into a single binary string or expression.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-704">並行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-704">concurrency</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-705">讓多位使用者同時存取和變更共用資料的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-705">A process that allows multiple users to access and change shared data at the same time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-706">Entity Framework 會實作開放式並行存取模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-706">The Entity Framework implements an optimistic concurrency model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-707">並行衝突</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-707">concurrency conflict</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-708">在兩個不同而之後同步處理的複本上變更相同的項目或變更單位時，所發生的衝突。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-708">A conflict that occurs when the same item or change unit is changed on two different replicas that are later synchronized.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-709">並行存取模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-709">concurrency model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-710">應用程式可設計為代表使用相同快取資料之並行作業的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-710">A way in which an application can be designed to account for concurrent operations that use the same cached data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-711">Windows Server AppFabric 支援開放式和封閉式並行存取模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-711">Windows Server AppFabric supports optimistic and pessimistic concurrency models.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-712">並行作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-712">concurrent operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-713">電腦作業，其中兩個或多個處理序 (程式) 可存取微處理器的時間，因此幾乎會同時執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-713">A computer operation in which two or more processes (programs) have access to the microprocessor's time and are therefore carried out nearly simultaneously.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-714">因為微處理器可以使用的時間單位小於人們可以察覺的時間單位，因此並行處理序幾乎是同時發生，但實際上並不是。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-714">Because a microprocessor can work with much smaller units of time than people can perceive, concurrent processes appear to be occurring simultaneously but in reality are not.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-715">條件運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-715">conditional expression</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-716">產生布林值 (true 或 false) 的運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-716">An expression that yields a Boolean value (true or false).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-717">這類運算式可能牽涉到比較 (測試值是否相等，或是針對非布林值， \< [less than] or > [大於] 關聯性) 和邏輯組合 (使用布林運算子，例如 and、or 和 XOR) 的布林運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-717">Such expressions can involve comparisons (testing values for equality or, for non-­Boolean values, the \< [less than] or > [greater than] relation) and logical combination (using Boolean operators such as AND, OR, and XOR) of Boolean expressions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-718">條件式分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-718">conditional split</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-719">完整資料庫備份、最新差異資料庫備份 (如果有的話)，以及在完整資料庫備份之後所建立之記錄備份 (如果有的話) 的還原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-719">A restore of a full database backup, the most recent differential database backup (if any), and the log backups (if any) taken since the full database backup.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-720">組態檔 (config file)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-720">config file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-721">一個檔案，其中包含一項硬體或軟體的電腦可讀取作業規格，或包含其他檔案或特定使用者的相關資訊 (例如使用者的登入 ID)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-721">A file that contains machine-readable operating specifications for a piece of hardware or software or that contains information on another file or on a specific user, such as the user's logon ID.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-722">組態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-722">configuration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-723">就單一微電腦而言，系統內部與外部元件的總和，包括記憶體、磁碟機、鍵盤、視訊，以及通常較不重要的附加元件硬體，例如滑鼠、數據機或印表機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-723">In reference to a single microcomputer, the sum of a system's internal and external components, including memory, disk drives, keyboard, video, and generally less critical add-on hardware, such as a mouse, modem, or printer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-724">需要軟體 (作業系統和各種裝置驅動程式)、使用者透過類似 IBM PC 和相容裝置上的 AUTOEXEC.BAT 和 CONFIG.SYS 檔案等組態檔所建立的選擇項目，以及某些時候的硬體 (交換器和跳接器)，才能設定組態正常運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-724">Software (the operating system and various device drivers), the user's choices established through configuration files such as the AUTOEXEC.BAT and CONFIG.SYS files on IBM PCs and compatibles, and sometimes hardware (switches and jumpers) are needed to "configure the configuration" to work correctly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-725">雖然系統組態可以變更 (增加更多的記憶體或磁碟容量)，但是系統的基本結構 (其架構) 維持不變。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-725">Although system configuration can be changed, as by adding more memory or disk capacity, the basic structure of the system--its architecture--remains the same.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-726">組態檔 (configuration file)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-726">configuration file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-727">一個檔案，其中包含一項硬體或軟體的電腦可讀取作業規格，或包含其他檔案或特定使用者的相關資訊 (例如使用者的登入 ID)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-727">A file that contains machine-readable operating specifications for a piece of hardware or software or that contains information on another file or on a specific user, such as the user's logon ID.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-728">組態工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-728">Configuration Tools</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-729">在 SQL Server 中，可讓使用者啟用、停用、啟動或停止 SQL Server 安裝功能、服務與遠端連接的功能表項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-729">In SQL Server, a menu item which allows the user to enable, disable, start, or stop the features, services, and remote connectivity of the SQL Server installations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-730">衝突偵測</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-730">conflict detection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-731">判斷某個複本已進行哪些作業而不知道有另一個複本存在的程序，例如當兩個複本都對相同項目進行本機更新時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-731">The process of determining which operations were made by one replica without knowledge of the other, such as when two replicas make local updates to the same item.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-732">衝突解決方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-732">conflict resolution method</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-733">用來判斷發生衝突時哪一項變更會寫入存放區的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-733">The method that is used to determine which change is written to the store in the event of a conflict.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-734">一般衝突解決方法如下：最後寫入者獲勝、來源獲勝、目的地獲勝、自訂或延後。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-734">Typical conflict resolution methods are as follows: last writer wins, source wins, destination wins, custom, or deferred.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-735">如果是自訂解決方法，解決的應用程式會從衝突記錄中讀取衝突，並選取解決方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-735">For custom resolution, the resolving application reads the conflict from the conflict log and selects a resolution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-736">如果是延後解決方法，衝突會連同衝突變更資料一起記錄，而且會在得知變更的情況下進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-736">For deferred resolution, the conflict is logged together with the conflicting change data and the made-with knowledge of the change.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-737">衝突解決器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-737">conflict resolver</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-738">處理衝突狀況解決的特殊機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-738">A special mechanism which handles resolving of conflict situations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-739">連接導向器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-739">Connection Director</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-740">連接技術，其中以不同資料存取技術 (.NET 或原生 Win32) 為基礎的應用程式可以共用相同的連接資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-740">A connectivity technology where applications based on different data access technologies (.NET or native Win32) can share the same connection information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-741">連接資訊可以針對這類用戶端應用程式集中管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-741">Connection information can be centrally managed for such client applications.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-742">連接管理員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-742">connection manager</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-743">執行階段連接到資料來源的邏輯表示法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-743">A logical representation of a run-time connection to a data source.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-744">連接字串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-744">connection string</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-745">一系列引數，定義資源的位置以及如何連接到該資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-745">A series of arguments that define the location of a resource and how to connect to it.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-746">一致性單位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-746">consistency unit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-747">資料同步處理的最小單位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-747">The minimal unit of data synchronization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-748">因為具有相同一致性單位的所有變更都會一起傳送，所以在套用一部分的一致性單位時，絕對不會中斷同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-748">Because all changes that have the same consistency unit are sent together, synchronization can never be interrupted with part of a consistency unit applied.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-749">常數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-749">constant</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-750">不需要計算，因此也不會變更的數值或字串值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-750">A numeric or string value that is not calculated and, therefore, does not change.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-751">條件約束衝突</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-751">constraint conflict</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-752">違反對項目或變更單位所加諸之條件約束的衝突，例如檔案系統內同名資料的資料夾或位置關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-752">A conflict that violates constraints that are put on items or change units, such as the relationship of folders or the location of identically-named data within a file system.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-753">強制違規</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-753">constraint violation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-754">未滿足限制準則時所發生的違規。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-754">A violation that occurs when the restriction criteria are not satisfied.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-755">自主資料庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-755">contained database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-756">SQL Server 資料庫，其中包含定義及存取資料庫所需的所有使用者驗證、資料庫設定和中繼資料，而且在組態上不會相依於資料庫安裝所在的 SQL Server Database Engine 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-756">A SQL Server database that includes all of the user authentication, database settings, and metadata required to define and access the database, and has no configuration dependencies on the instance of the SQL Server Database Engine where the database is installed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-757">容器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-757">container</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-758">提供封裝結構的控制流程元素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-758">A control flow element that provides package structure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-759">內容格式器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-759">content formatter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-760">散發者的一部分，它會將原始通知資料轉換成可讀取的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-760">The part of the distributor that turns raw notification data into readable messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-761">內容金鑰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-761">content key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-762">在發行和耗用期間用來加密和解密受保護內容的密碼編譯金鑰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-762">The cryptographic key used to both encrypt and decrypt protected content during publishing and consumption.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-763">競爭</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-763">contention</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-764">網路上工作站之間的競爭，以取得使用通訊線路或網路資源的機會。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-764">On a network, competition among stations for the opportunity to use a communications line or network resource.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-765">內容窗格</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-765">Context pane</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-766">資料表設計工具中包含的樹狀檢視，此檢視會列出與資料表相關的物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-766">A tree view included in the Table Designer that lists objects related to a table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-767">環境切換 (context switch)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-767">context switch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-768">指根據檢查哪些權限可執行陳述式或執行動作的結果來變更識別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-768">The changing of the identity against which permissions to execute statements or perform actions are checked.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-769">接續媒體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-769">continuation media</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-770">在最初媒體已滿之後所使用的卸除式備份媒體系列，可允許持續進行備份作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-770">The series of removable backup media used after the initial medium becomes full, allowing continuation of the backup operation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-771">接續磁帶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-771">continuation tape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-772">在媒體系列中的最初磁帶填滿之後使用的磁帶，以便接續媒體系列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-772">A tape that is used after the initial tape in a media family fills, allowing continuation of a media family.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-773">合約</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-773">contract</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-774">定義可在給定交談中交換之訊息類型的 Service Broker 物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-774">A Service Broker object that defines the message types that can be exchanged within a given conversation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-775">控制流程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-775">control flow</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-776">一組連接且執行工作的控制流程元素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-776">A group of connected control flow elements that perform tasks.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-777">control-break 報表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-777">control-break report</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-778">摘要列出使用者定義群組或分頁中之資料的報表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-778">A report that summarizes data in user-defined groups or breaks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-779">遇到不同的資料時，就會觸發新的群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-779">A new group is triggered when different data is encountered.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-780">流程控制語言</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-780">control-of-flow language</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-781">一些 Transact-SQL 關鍵字，用於控制觸發程序、預存程序和批次中 SQL 陳述式和陳述式區塊的執行流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-781">Transact-SQL keywords that control the flow of execution of SQL statements and statement blocks in triggers, stored procedures, and batches.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-782">交談端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-782">conversation endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-783">代表參與交談之對象的物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-783">The object which represents a party participating in the conversation.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-877">資料字典</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-877">data dictionary</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-878">包含資料庫系統中所有資料庫相關資料的資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-878">A database containing data about all the databases in a database system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-879">資料字典會儲存所有各種不同的結構描述和檔案規格與其位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-879">Data dictionaries store all the various schema and file specifications and their locations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-880">也會包含哪些程式使用哪些資料以及哪些使用者對於哪些報表有興趣的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-880">They also contain information about which programs use which data and which users are interested in which reports.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-883">資料爆炸</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-883">data explosion</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-884">指多維度結構 (如 Cube) 的大小因儲存彙總資料而呈指數成長。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-884">The exponential growth in size of a multidimensional structure, such as a cube, due to the storage of aggregated data.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-903">資料超市</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-903">data mart</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-904">資料倉儲內容的子集，其中包含的資料通常會著重於部門層級或是特定的商業領域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-904">A subset of the contents of a data warehouse that tends to contain data focused at the department level, or on a specific business area.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-955">資料庫圖表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-955">database diagram</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-956">資料庫結構描述中任何部分的圖形表示法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-956">A graphical representation of any portion of a database schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-957">這可以是資料庫結構的全貌或部分面貌。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-957">It can be either a whole or partial picture of the structure of the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-958">其中包括資料表、資料表所包含的資料行，以及資料表之間的關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-958">It includes tables, the columns they contain, and the relationships between the tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-959">資料庫引擎</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-959">database engine</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-960">可讓您存取資料庫管理系統 (DBMS) 的程式模組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-960">The program module or modules that provide access to a database management system (DBMS).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-961">Database Engine Tuning Advisor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-961">Database Engine Tuning Advisor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-962">用來微調實體資料庫設計的工具，可幫助使用者選取及建立一組最佳的索引、索引檢視表和資料分割。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-962">A tool for tuning the physical database design that helps users to select and create an optimal set of indexes, indexed views, and partitioning.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-975">資料庫鏡像</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-975">database mirroring</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-976">這項程序會立即將讀取/寫入資料庫 (主體資料庫) 的每項更新重製到 Database Engine 個別執行個體 (鏡像伺服器) 上的資料庫唯讀鏡像 (鏡像資料庫)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-976">Immediately reproducing every update to a read-write database (the principal database) onto a read-only mirror of that database (the mirror database) residing on a separate instance of the database engine (the mirror server).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-977">在實際執行環境中，鏡像伺服器位於另一部電腦上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-977">In production environments, the mirror server is on another machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-978">鏡像資料庫是在不復原的情況下，藉由還原主體資料庫的完整備份所建立的一種資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-978">The mirror database is created by restoring a full backup of the principal database (without recovery).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-979">資料庫鏡像監視器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-979">Database Mirroring Monitor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-980">用來監控伺服器執行個體上任何鏡像資料庫子集的工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-980">A tool used to monitor any subset of the mirrored databases on a server instance.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1019">DBCS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1019">DBCS</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1020">可使用一個以上的位元組代表單一字元的字元集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1020">A character set that can use more than one byte to represent a single character.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1021">DBCS 包括由 1 個位元組所組成的某些字元以及由 2 個位元組所組成的某些字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1021">A DBCS includes some characters that consist of 1 byte and some characters that consist of 2 bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1022">類似中文、日文和韓文的語言都使用 DBCS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1022">Languages such as Chinese, Japanese, and Korean use DBCS.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1023">DBMS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1023">DBMS</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1024">實體資料庫與使用者之間的軟體層。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1024">A layer of software between the physical database and the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1025">DBMS 會管理資料庫的所有存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1025">The DBMS manages all access to the database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1026">DDL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1026">DDL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1027">定義資料庫的所有屬性 (Attribute) 和屬性 (Property) 的語言，特別是記錄配置、欄位定義、索引鍵欄位、檔案位置和儲存策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1027">A language that defines all attributes and properties of a database, especially record layouts, field definitions, key fields, file locations, and storage strategy.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1028">DDL 觸發程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1028">DDL trigger</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1029">特殊類型的觸發程序，它會為了回應「資料定義語言」(Data Definition Language，DDL) 陳述式而執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1029">A special kind of trigger that executes in response to Data Definition Language (DDL) statements.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1030">deadlock</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1030">deadlock</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1031">各鎖定一段資料的兩位使用者試圖取得另一方資料片段的鎖定狀況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1031">A situation when two users, each having a lock on one piece of data, attempt to acquire a lock on the other's piece.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1034">決策樹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1034">decision tree</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1035">特定資料採礦方法所產生之資料的樹狀模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1035">A treelike model of data produced by certain data mining methods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1036">決策樹可用於預測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1036">Decision trees can be used for prediction.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1037">宣告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1037">declaration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1038">將識別項繫結至與其相關的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1038">A binding of an identifier to the information that relates to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1039">例如，為了讓常數的宣告繫結包含值的常數名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1039">For example, to make a declaration of a constant means to bind the name of the constant with its value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1040">宣告通常會發生在程式的原始程式碼內，實際的繫結會發生在編譯時間或執行階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1040">Declaration usually occurs in a program's source code; the actual binding can take place at compile time or run time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1041">宣告式管理架構</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1041">Declarative Management Framework</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1042">以原則為基礎的 SQL Server 管理系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1042">A policy based system of SQL Server management.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1043">宣告式管理架構 Facet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1043">Declarative Management Framework Facet</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1044">一組預先定義的邏輯屬性，可在以原則為基礎的管理中將某些類型的受管理目標 (例如資料庫、資料表、登入、檢視等) 的行為或特性模型化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1044">A set of logical pre-defined properties that model the behavior or characteristics for certain types of managed targets (such as a database, table, login, view,etc) in policy-based management.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1045">宣告式參考完整性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1045">declarative referential integrity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1046">定義為資料表定義之一部分的 FOREIGN KEY 條件約束，可強制施行資料表之間的適當關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1046">FOREIGN KEY constraints defined as part of a table definition that enforce proper relationships between tables.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1135">維度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1135">dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1136">將資料組織成層級之 Cube 的結構性屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1136">A structural attribute of a cube that organizes data into levels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1137">例如，Geography 維度可能包含 Country、Region、State 或 Province 和 City 等成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1137">For example, a Geography dimension might include the members Country, Region, State or Province, and City.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1138">維度運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1138">dimension expression</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1139">傳回維度的有效多維度運算式 (MDX) 運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1139">A valid Multidimensional Expressions (MDX) expression that returns a dimension.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1140">維度資料粒度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1140">dimension granularity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1141">相對於特定量值群組而言，可供特定維度使用的最低層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1141">The lowest level available to a particular dimension in relation to a particular measure group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1142">「自然」或實體粒度一定是索引鍵的粒度，可將主要維度資料表聯結到主要事實資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1142">The "natural" or physical grain is always that of the key that joins the main dimension table to the primary fact table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1143">維度階層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1143">dimension hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1144">一種邏輯樹狀結構，它將維度的各個成員組織起來，使每個成員都有一個父成員及零或多個子成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1144">A logical tree structure that organizes the members of a dimension such that each member has one parent member and zero or more child members.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1145">維度層級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1145">dimension level</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1146">維度階層中一組成員的名稱，這個組的所有成員與階層根的距離都相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1146">The name of a set of members in a dimension hierarchy such that all members of the set are at the same distance from the root of the hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1147">例如，時間階層可能包含年、月和日層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1147">For example, a time hierarchy may contain the levels Year, Month, and Day.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1148">維度成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1148">dimension member</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1149">維度中的單一位置或項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1149">A single position or item in a dimension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1150">維度成員可以是使用者定義或預先定義，而且可以擁有相關聯的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1150">Dimension members can be user-defined or predefined and can have properties associated with them.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1151">維度成員屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1151">dimension member property</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1152">維度成員的特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1152">A characteristic of a dimension member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1153">維度成員屬性可以是英數、布林或日期/時間資料類型，而且可以是使用者定義或預先定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1153">Dimension member properties can be alphanumeric, Boolean, or Date/Time data types, and can be user-defined or predefined.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1154">維度資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1154">dimension table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1155">資料倉儲中的資料表，其項目用於描述事實資料表中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1155">A table in a data warehouse whose entries describe data in a fact table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1156">直接連接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1156">direct connect</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1157">連接到後端資料庫的狀態，當您儲存圖表或其中的選定項目時，您在資料庫圖表中進行的任何變更都會自動更新您的資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1157">The state of being connected to a back-end database, so that any changes you make to a database diagram automatically update your database when you save the diagram or selected items in it.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1158">直接回應模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1158">direct response mode</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1159">在 SQL Server 統計資料顯示之外，個別收集 SQL Server 統計資料的預設模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1159">The default mode in which SQL Server statistics are gathered separately from the SQL Server Statistics display.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1160">中途分頁</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1160">dirty page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1161">包含尚未寫入磁碟之修改的緩衝區頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1161">A buffer page that contains modifications that have not been written to disk.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1162">中途讀取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1162">dirty read</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1163">包含未認可資料的讀取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1163">A read that contains uncommitted data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1164">停用的索引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1164">disabled index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1165">已標示為停用的任何索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1165">Any index that has been marked as disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1166">停用的索引無法提供給 Database Engine 使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1166">A disabled index is unavailable for use by the database engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1167">已停用之索引的索引定義會保留在系統目錄中，但不含基礎索引資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1167">The index definition of a disabled index remains in the system catalog with no underlying index data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1168">離散訊號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1168">discrete signal</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1169">由一連串數量組成的時間序列，此時間序列是離散整數範圍的函數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1169">A time series consisting of a sequence of quantities, that is a time series that is a function over a domain of discrete integers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1170">離散化</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1170">discretize</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1171">將連續資料集的值放入群組中，以便產生離散數目的可能狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1171">To put values of a continuous set of data into groups so that there are a discrete number of possible states.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1172">離散化資料行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1172">discretized column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1173">這是代表有限計算資料的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1173">A column that represents finite, counted data</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1174">相異計數量值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1174">distinct count measure</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1175">此量值通常用來針對維度的每一個成員判斷，另一個維度有多少相異的最低層級成員共用事實資料表中的資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1175">A measure commonly used to determine for each member of a dimension how many distinct, lowest-level members of another dimension share rows in the fact table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1176">分散式資料分割檢視</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1176">distributed partitioned view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1177">聯結跨越一部以上伺服器的一組成員資料表之水平資料分割資料的檢視，讓資料顯示成來自某份資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1177">A view that joins horizontally partitioned data from a set of member tables across more than one server, making the data appear as if from one table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1178">分散式查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1178">distributed query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1179">存取多個資料來源之資料的單一查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1179">A single query that accesses data from multiple data sources.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1180">分散式交易</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1180">distributed transaction</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1181">跨越多個資料來源的交易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1181">A transaction that spans multiple data sources.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1182">distribution cleanup agent</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1182">distribution cleanup agent</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1183">在 SQL Server Agent 底下執行的排程作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1183">A scheduled job that runs under SQL Server Agent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1184">在所有訂閱者都收到交易之後，此代理程式會從散發資料庫中移除交易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1184">After all Subscribers have received a transaction, the agent removes the transaction from the distribution database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1185">當從散發資料庫中移除與這些檔案對應的項目之後，它也會從檔案系統中清除快照集檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1185">It also cleans up snapshot files from the file system after entries corresponding to those files have been removed from the distribution database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1186">distribution database</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1186">distribution database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1187">散發者端的資料庫，可儲存複寫的資料，包括交易、快照集作業、同步處理狀態和複寫記錄資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1187">A database on the Distributor that stores data for replication including transactions, snapshot jobs, synchronization status, and replication history information.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1188">散發保留週期</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1188">distribution retention period</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1189">在異動複寫中，交易儲存在散發資料庫中的時間量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1189">In transactional replication, the amount of time transactions are stored in the distribution database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1190">distributor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1190">distributor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1191">資料庫執行個體，用於當做與一個或多個發行者相關聯之特定複寫資料的存放區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1191">A database instance that acts as a store for replication-specific data associated with one or more Publishers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1192">DMF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1192">DMF</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1193">一組內建函數的其中一個，可傳回 SQL Server 中有關值、物件和設定的伺服器狀態資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1193">One of a set of built-in functions that returns server state information about values, objects, and settings in SQL Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1194">DML</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1194">DML</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1195">用於擷取和操作資料的 SQL 陳述式子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1195">The subset of SQL statements that is used to retrieve and manipulate data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1196">DML 陳述式通常會以 SELECT INSERT UPDATE 或 DELETE 當做開頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1196">DML statements typically start with SELECT INSERT UPDATE or DELETE.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1197">DML 觸發程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1197">DML trigger</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1198">修改指定資料表的資料時所執行的預存程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1198">A stored procedure that executes when data in a specified table is modified.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1203">網域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1203">domain</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1204">可為函數中的獨立變數或資料庫屬性指定的一組可能值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1204">The set of possible values that you can specify for an independent variable in a function, or for a database attribute.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1205">網域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1205">domain</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1206">網路環境中共用共同的資料庫、目錄資料庫或樹狀結構的電腦集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1206">A collection of computers in a networked environment that share a common database, directory database, or tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1207">網域會當做具有共同規則與程序的一個單位來管理 (其中包含安全性原則)，而且每一個網域都有唯一的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1207">A domain is administered as a unit with common rules and procedures, which can include security policies, and each domain has a unique name.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1208">網域環境</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1208">domain context</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1209">網域服務的用戶端表示法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1209">A client-side representation of a domain service.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1210">值域完整性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1210">domain integrity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1211">特定資料行的項目有效性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1211">The validity of entries for a specific column of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1212">網域作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1212">domain operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1213">網域服務上對用戶端應用程式公開的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1213">A method on a domain service that is exposed to a client application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1214">它可讓用戶端應用程式在實體上執行動作，例如查詢、更新、插入或刪除記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1214">It enables client applications to perform an action on the entity such as, query, update, insert, or delete records.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1215">網域服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1215">domain service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1216">封裝應用程式之商務邏輯的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1216">A service that encapsulates the business logic of an application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1217">它會公開服務層中一組相關的網域作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1217">It exposes a set of related domain operations in a service layer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1218">休眠工作階段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1218">dormant session</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1219">預先登入狀態中的工作階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1219">Session in pre-login state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1220">您可以啟動或結束工作階段以修改其狀態，但通常會維持在「睡眠/閒置」狀態 (例如，已啟動工作階段並已在伺服器開啟工作階段供用戶端使用)，或維持在「休眠」狀態 (例如，已結束工作階段且伺服器目前沒有工作階段供用戶端使用)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1220">Sessions can be initiated or ended to modify their state, but they generally remain in either a "sleep/idle" state, such as when the session has been initiated and is open at the server for client use; or a "dormant" state, such as when the session has been ended and the session is not currently available at the server for client use.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1221">雙位元組字集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1221">double byte character set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1222">可使用一個以上的位元組代表單一字元的字元集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1222">A character set that can use more than one byte to represent a single character.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1223">DBCS 包括由 1 個位元組所組成的某些字元以及由 2 個位元組所組成的某些字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1223">A DBCS includes some characters that consist of 1 byte and some characters that consist of 2 bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1224">類似中文、日文和韓文的語言都使用 DBCS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1224">Languages such as Chinese, Japanese, and Korean use DBCS.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1225">雙位元組字集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1225">double-byte character set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1226">可使用一個以上的位元組代表單一字元的字元集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1226">A character set that can use more than one byte to represent a single character.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1227">DBCS 包括由 1 個位元組所組成的某些字元以及由 2 個位元組所組成的某些字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1227">A DBCS includes some characters that consist of 1 byte and some characters that consist of 2 bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1228">類似中文、日文和韓文的語言都使用 DBCS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1228">Languages such as Chinese, Japanese, and Korean use DBCS.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1435">指數移動平均</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1435">exponential moving average</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1436">資料移動平均值，它會對期間內較新的資料給予較多的加權，並對期間內較舊的資料給予較少的加權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1436">A moving average of data that gives more weight to the more recent data in the period and less weight to the older data in the period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1437">此公式會套用加權因數，加權因數會以指數方式遞減。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1437">The formula applies weighting factors which decrease exponentially.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1438">每一個較舊資料點的加權都會以指數方式遞減，為較新的觀察給予更高的重要性，同時不會完全捨棄較舊的觀察。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1438">The weighting for each older data point decreases exponentially, giving much more importance to recent observations while still not discarding older observations entirely.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1487">容錯移轉</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1487">fail over</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1488">將失敗的元件切換處理為其備用元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1488">To switch processing from a failed component to its backup component.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1491">容錯移轉叢集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1491">failover cluster</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1492">位於一個位置而且透過網路連接在一起的一組伺服器，其目的是為了在伺服器失敗時提供即時備援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1492">A group of servers that are in one location and that are networked together for the purpose of providing live backup in case one of the servers fails.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1522">檔案差異備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1522">file differential backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1523">一個或多個檔案的備份，其中僅包含自從最近的檔案備份以來，對每個檔案所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1523">A backup of one or more files containing only changes made to each file since its most recent file backup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1524">檔案差異備份需要以完整檔案備份當做基底。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1524">A file differential backup requires a full file backup as a base.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1525">檔案 DSN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1525">file DSN</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1526">檔案資料來源名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1526">file Data Source Names.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1527">安裝相同驅動程式的所有使用者會共用以檔案為基礎的資料來源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1527">File-based data sources shared among all users with the same drivers installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1528">這些資料來源並非某位使用者專用或某部電腦本機使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1528">These data sources are not dedicated to a user or local to a computer.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1535">filegroup</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1535">filegroup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1536">構成單一資料配置單位或用於資料庫管理的一個或多個資料檔案的具名集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1536">A named collection of one or more data files that forms a single unit of data allocation or for administration of a database.</span></span>|
