|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1541">填滿因數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1541">fill factor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1542">索引屬性，用於定義 SQL Server Database Engine 應該使每個索引頁面填滿的程度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1542">An attribute of an index that defines how full the SQL Server Database Engine should make each page of the index.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1543">篩選忘記的知識</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1543">filter forgotten knowledge</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1544">用來當做篩選追蹤起點的知識。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1544">The knowledge that is used as the starting point for filter tracking.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1545">篩選追蹤複本可以節省儲存空間，其方法是移除棄置項目，並推進篩選忘記的知識，以便容納已經移除之棄置項目的最高版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1545">A filter-tracking replica can save storage space by removing ghosts and advancing the filter forgotten knowledge to contain the highest version of the ghosts that have been removed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1546">篩選索引鍵</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1546">filter key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1547">一個 4 位元組的值，它會對應到篩選索引鍵對應中的篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1547">A 4-byte value that maps to a filter in a filter key map.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1548">篩選的複本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1548">filtered replica</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1549">只儲存篩選中項目之項目資料的複本，例如，只會儲存評分為三顆星 (含) 以上之歌曲的媒體儲存複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1549">A replica that stores item data only for items that are in a filter, such as a media storage replica that stores only songs that are rated as three stars or better.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1550">篩選追蹤複本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1550">filter-tracking replica</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1551">可以識別哪些項目在篩選中以及哪些項目最近從篩選中移出或移入的複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1551">A replica that can identify which items are in a filter and which have moved in or out of the filter recently.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1552">細部鎖定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1552">fine-grained lock</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1553">適用於少量程式碼或資料的鎖定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1553">A lock that applies to a small amount of code or data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1554">調整</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1554">fit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1555">用來評估資料採礦演算法是否成功的其中一個準則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1555">One of the criteria used for evaluating the success of a data mining algorithm.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1556">調整通常會表示為 0 與 1 之間的值，而且其計算方式是取得評估案例的預測值與實際值之間的共變數，並除以相同預測值和實際值的標準差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1556">Fit is typically represented as a value between 0 and 1, and is calculated by taking the covariance between the predicted and actual values of evaluated cases and dividing by the standard deviations of the same predicted and actual values.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1557">固定資料庫角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1557">fixed database role</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1558">存在每個資料庫中的預先定義角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1558">A predefined role that exists in each database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1559">此角色的範圍會限制為它所定義的資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1559">The scope of the role is limited to the database in which it is defined.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1560">固定伺服器角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1560">fixed server role</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1561">存在伺服器層級的預先定義角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1561">A predefined role that exists at the server level.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1562">此角色的範圍會限制為其定義所在的 SQL Server 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1562">The scope of the role is limited to the SQL Server instance in which it is defined.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1563">FK</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1563">FK</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1564">資料庫資料表中的索引鍵，它來自於另一個資料表 (也稱為「參考資料表」) 而且它的值符合參考資料表中的主索引鍵 (PK) 或唯一索引鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1564">A key in a database table that comes from another table (also know as the "referenced table") and whose values match the primary key (PK) or unique key in the referenced table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1565">一般檔案 (flat file)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1565">flat file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1566">包含單一記錄類型之記錄的檔案，其中沒有管理記錄之間關聯性的內嵌結構資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1566">A file consisting of records of a single record type in which there is no embedded structure information that governs relationships between records.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1567">扁平化</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1567">flatten</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1568">將巢狀結構轉換成扁平結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1568">To convert a nested structure into a flat structure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1569">扁平化介面</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1569">flattened interface</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1570">為了結合多介面的各個成員而建立的介面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1570">An interface created to combine members of multiple interfaces.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1571">扁平化資料列集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1571">flattened rowset</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1572">以兩個維度的資料列集來表現的多維度資料集，多維度元素的唯一組合會結合在一個軸上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1572">A multidimensional data set presented as a two-dimensional rowset in which unique combinations of elements of multiple dimensions are combined on an axis.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1573">彈性識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1573">flexible ID</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1574">指派給各種不同同步處理實體 (例如複本) 的識別碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1574">An identifier that is assigned to various synchronization entities, such as replicas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1575">此識別碼可以是固定或變動長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1575">The identifier can be of fixed or variable length.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1576">彈性識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1576">flexible identifier</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1577">指派給各種不同同步處理實體 (例如複本) 的識別碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1577">An identifier that is assigned to various synchronization entities, such as replicas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1578">此識別碼可以是固定或變動長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1578">The identifier can be of fixed or variable length.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1579">摺疊計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1579">fold count</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1580">表示在原始資料集內建立之資料分割數目的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1580">A value that represents the number of partitions that will be created within the original data set.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1581">資料夾階層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1581">folder hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1582">可唯一識別下列項目的有界限命名空間：儲存在報表伺服器中並由其管理的所有報表、資料夾、共用資料來源項目以及資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1582">A bounded namespace that uniquely identifies all reports, folders, shared data source items, and resources that are stored in and managed by a report server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1583">強制的服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1583">forced service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1584">在資料庫鏡像工作階段中，資料庫擁有者在主體伺服器失敗時所起始的容錯移轉，它會將服務傳送至鏡像資料庫 (處於未知狀態)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1584">In a database mirroring session, a failover initiated by the database owner upon the failure of the principal server that transfers service to the mirror database while it is in an unknown state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1585">資料可能會遺失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1585">Data may be lost.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1586">外部索引鍵 (foreign key)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1586">foreign key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1587">資料庫資料表中的索引鍵，它來自於另一個資料表 (也稱為「參考資料表」) 而且它的值符合參考資料表中的主索引鍵 (PK) 或唯一索引鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1587">A key in a database table that comes from another table (also know as the "referenced table") and whose values match the primary key (PK) or unique key in the referenced table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1588">外部索引鍵關聯</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1588">foreign key association</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1589">透過外部索引鍵屬性管理之實體之間的關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1589">An association between entities that is managed through foreign key properties.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1590">外部資料表 (foreign table)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1590">foreign table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1591">包含外部索引鍵的資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1591">A table that contains a foreign key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1592">格式檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1592">format file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1593">包含從資料檔讀取資料或將資料寫入其中時用於解譯資料之中繼資訊 (例如資料類型和資料行大小) 的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1593">A file containing meta information (such as data type and column size) that is used to interpret data when being read from or written to a data file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1594">順向資料指標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1594">forward-only cursor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1595">無法捲動的資料指標；資料列只能依照從第一列到最後一列的順序閱讀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1595">A cursor that cannot be scrolled; rows can be read only in sequence from the first row to the last row.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1596">自由格式語言</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1596">free-form language</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1597">語法未受到字元在某一行的位置所限制的語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1597">A language whose syntax is not constrained by the position of characters on a line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1598">C 和 Pascal 為自由格式語言，FORTRAN 則不是。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1598">C and Pascal are free-form languages; FORTRAN is not.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1599">完整備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1599">full backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1600">整個資料庫的備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1600">A backup of an entire database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1601">完整差異備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1601">full differential backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1602">資料庫中所有檔案的備份，其中僅包含自從最近的完整備份以來，對資料庫所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1602">A backup of all files in the database, containing only changes made to the database since the most recent full backup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1603">完整差異備份需要以完整備份當做基底。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1603">A full differential backup requires a full backup as a base.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1604">完整外部聯結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1604">full outer join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1605">外部聯結類型，這種聯結類型會併入所有聯結的資料表中的所有資料列，不論它們是否符合都是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1605">A type of outer join in which all rows in all joined tables are included, whether they are matched or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1606">例如，標題和發行者之間的完整外部聯結將顯示所有標題和所有發行者，即使它們並不相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1606">For example, a full outer join between titles and publishers shows all titles and all publishers, even those that have no match.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1607">完整復原模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1607">full recovery model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1608">資料庫復原模式，它會完整記錄所有交易，而且會將所有記錄保留到全部都備份完成為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1608">A database recovery mode that fully logs all transactions and retains all the log records until after they are backed up.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1609">如果在失敗之後備份記錄結尾，則資料庫可以復原到失敗點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1609">The database can be recovered to the point of failure if the tail of the log is backed up after the failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1610">所有形式的復原都有支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1610">All forms of recovery are supported.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1611">全文檢索目錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1611">full-text catalog</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1612">全文檢索索引元件和其他檔案的集合，這些會在特定的目錄結構中組織，並包含執行查詢所需的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1612">A collection of full-text index components and other files that are organized in a specific directory structure and contain the data that is needed to perform queries.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1613">啟用全文檢索功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1613">full-text enabling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1614">允許全文檢索查詢在目前資料庫上發生的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1614">The process of allowing full-text querying to occur on the current database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1615">全文檢索查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1615">full-text query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1616">做為一個 SELECT 陳述式，一種會在字元型資料行 (char、varchar、text、ntext、nchar 或 nvarchar 等資料類型) 中搜尋單字、片語或多種單字或片語形式的查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1616">As a SELECT statement, a query that searches for words, phrases, or multiple forms of a word or phrase in the character-based columns (of char, varchar, text, ntext, nchar, or nvarchar data types).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1617">SELECT 陳述式會傳回符合搜尋準則的資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1617">The SELECT statement returns those rows meeting the search criteria.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1618">全文檢索搜尋</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1618">full-text search</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1619">指根據所有實際文字資料而非包含有限關鍵字集的索引，搜尋一個或多個文件、記錄或字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1619">A search for one or more documents, records, or strings based on all of the actual text data rather than on an index containing a limited set of keywords.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1620">全文檢索服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1620">Full-Text service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1621">會執行全文檢索查詢的 SQL Server 元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1621">The SQL Server component that performs the full-text querying.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1622">全形字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1622">full-width character</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1623">在雙位元組字集中，由 2 個位元組所表示而且通常具有半形變化的字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1623">In a double-byte character set, a character that is represented by 2 bytes and typically has a half-width variant.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1624">函數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1624">function</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1625">做為單一邏輯單元來運作的一段程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1625">A piece of code that operates as a single logical unit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1626">函數依名稱來呼叫，它會接受選擇性的輸入參數，且會傳回狀態和選擇性的輸出參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1626">A function is called by name, accepts optional input parameters, and returns a status and optional output parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1627">許多程式語言都支援函數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1627">Many programming languages support functions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1628">模糊群組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1628">fuzzy grouping</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1629">在 Integration Services 中的資料清除方法，該方法會檢查資料集中的各個值，也會識別相關資料列的群組以及做為群組標準表示法的一個資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1629">In Integration Services, a data cleaning methodology that examines values in a dataset and identifies groups of related data rows and the one data row that is the canonical representation of the group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1630">模糊比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1630">fuzzy matching</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1631">Integration Services 中的查閱方法，該方法會使用近似比對演算法來尋找參考資料表中的類似資料值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1631">In Integration Services, a lookup methodology that uses an approximate matching algorithm to locate similar data values in a reference table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1632">GAC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1632">GAC</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1633">整個電腦的程式碼快取，它會存放供電腦上多個應用程式共用而特別安裝的組件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1633">A computer-wide code cache that stores assemblies specifically installed to be shared by many applications on the computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1634">間隙深度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1634">gap depth</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1635">指定沿著不同資料列顯示之資料數列間的距離，當做叢集結果的量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1635">A measure that specifies the distance between data series that are displayed along distinct rows, as a result of clustering.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1636">記憶體回收</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1636">garbage collection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1637">自動復原堆積記憶體的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1637">A process for automatic recovery of heap memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1638">已配置但不再使用的記憶體區塊將會釋出，而且可能會移動仍在使用中的記憶體區塊，以便將可用的記憶體合併成較大的區塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1638">Blocks of memory that had been allocated but are no longer in use are freed, and blocks of memory still in use may be moved to consolidate the free memory into larger blocks.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1639">記憶體回收行程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1639">garbage collector</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1640">執行記憶體回收的作業系統部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1640">The part of the operating system that performs garbage collection.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1641">閘門守護式連結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1641">gated link</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1642">兩個或多個物件之間的受保護連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1642">A protected link between two or more objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1643">在執行期間，一旦建立了物件關聯性，就不會檢查該物件關聯性兩端的權限，而且不必多次檢查認證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1643">During execution, permissions are not checked across the object relationship once it has been established and credentials don't have to be checked several times.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1644">當提供權限給許多相依物件的作業不適合進行或無法管理時，這種連結類型就很有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1644">This type of link is useful when it is not appropriate or manageable to give permissions to many dependent objects.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1645">累積寫出作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1645">gather-write operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1646">效能最佳化方式，其中 Database Engine 會將多個修改過的資料頁面收集到單一寫入作業中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1646">A performance optimization where the Database Engine collects multiple modified data pages into a single write operation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1647">GC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1647">GC</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1648">自動復原堆積記憶體的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1648">A process for automatic recovery of heap memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1649">已配置但不再使用的記憶體區塊將會釋出，而且可能會移動仍在使用中的記憶體區塊，以便將可用的記憶體合併成較大的區塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1649">Blocks of memory that had been allocated but are no longer in use are freed, and blocks of memory still in use may be moved to consolidate the free memory into larger blocks.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1650">產生的程式碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1650">generated code</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1651">當伺服器和用戶端專案之間有 RIA Services 連結存在時，根據中間層所公開的作業和實體自動為用戶端專案產生的程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1651">Code that is automatically generated for the client project based on operations and entities exposed in the middle tier when a RIA Services link exists between the server and client projects.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1658">棄置項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1658">ghost</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1659">篩選的複本中的項目或變更單位，該項目或單位已在篩選內或是已經移出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1659">An item or change unit in a filtered replica that was in the filter and has moved out.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1660">準刪除記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1660">ghost record</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1661">在索引的分葉層級中，已經標示要刪除但是尚未由資料庫引擎刪除的資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1661">Row in the leaf level of an index that has been marked for deletion, but has not yet been deleted by the database engine.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1668">全域識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1668">global ID</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1669">指派給資料項目的唯一識別碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1669">A unique identifier that is assigned to a data item.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1670">此識別碼必須跨越所有用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1670">The identifier must be unique across all clients.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1671">全域識別碼是一個彈性的識別碼，所以可以是任何格式，而且通常是 GUID 和 8 位元組的前置詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1671">A global identifier is a flexible identifier and so can be any format, but it is typically a GUID and an 8-byte prefix.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1683">資料粒度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1683">granularity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1684">電腦活動或功能的描述，從「粗略」到「精細」(例如螢幕解析度、搜尋和排序或是時間配量配置)，這是根據它所處理的單位大小 (像素、資料集或時間配量)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1684">A description, from "coarse" to "fine", of a computer activity or feature (such as screen resolution, searching and sorting, or time slice allocation) in terms of the size of the units it handles (pixels, sets of data, or time slices).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1685">當片段越大時，資料粒度也會越粗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1685">The larger the pieces, the coarser the granularity.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1712">雜湊分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1712">hash partitioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1713">分割資料表或索引的一種方式，其方法是根據指定的資料分割數目以及一個或多個分割資料行的值，允許 SQL Server 將內部雜湊演算法套用到橫跨資料分割的廣大資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1713">A way of partitioning a table or index by allowing SQL Server to apply an internal hash algorithm to spread rows across partitions based on the number of partitions specified and the values of one or more partitioning columns.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1714">熱門地圖 (heat map)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1714">heat map</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1715">一種地圖表示法，其中每個多邊形的色彩濃度都會對應到相關的分析資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1715">A type of map presentation where the intensity of color for each polygon corresponds to the related analytical data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1716">例如，範圍中較小的值會以藍色 (冷門) 顯示，而較大的值則以紅色 (熱門) 顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1716">For example, low values in a range appear as blue (cold) and high values as red (hot).</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1725">高可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1725">high availability</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1726">在需要時能夠使用系統或裝置的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1726">The ability of a system or device to be usable when it is needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1727">當以百分比表示時，高可用性是實際服務時間除以所需的服務時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1727">When expressed as a percentage, high availability is the actual service time divided by the required service time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1728">雖然高可用性不保證系統沒有停機時間，但是如果到達百分之 99.999 的網路執行時間，網路通常就會視為高可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1728">Although high availability does not guarantee that a system will have no downtime, a network often is considered highly available if it achieves 99.999 percent network uptime.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1729">上限標準</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1729">high watermark</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1730">每一部快取主機上的記憶體耗用量臨界值，可指定何時從記憶體收回物件，不論物件是否已過期，直到記憶體耗用量回到下限標準為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1730">A memory consumption threshold on each cache host that specifies when objects are evicted out of memory, regardless of whether they have expired or not, until memory consumption goes back down to the low watermark.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1809">內送郵件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1809">incoming message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1810">橫跨一個或多個郵件系統傳送的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1810">A message that has been sent across one or more messaging systems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1811">它可能只傳送給您或是其他多個收件者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1811">It may have been sent only to you or to many other recipients.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1812">內送郵件會放置在接收資料夾中，該資料夾是指定來保存特定類別的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1812">Incoming messages are placed in a receive folder designated to hold messages of a particular class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1813">您可以針對您處理的每一個郵件類別設定不同的接收資料夾，或者可以針對所有類別使用一個資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1813">You can set up a different receive folder for each message class that you handle or use one folder for all of the classes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1814">累加式更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1814">incremental update</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1815">一組將新成員加入現有 Cube 或維度，或將新資料加入資料分割的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1815">The set of operations that either adds new members to an existing cube or dimension, or adds new data to a partition.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1816">獨立關聯</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1816">independent association</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1817">實體之間以獨立物件表示及追蹤的關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1817">An association between entities that is represented and tracked by an independent object.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1818">索引配置對應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1818">Index Allocation Map</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1819">對應配置單位所使用之資料庫檔案內 4 GB 部分範圍的頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1819">A page that maps the extents in a 4-GB part of a database file that is used by an allocation unit.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1820">索引頁</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1820">index page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1821">包含索引資料列的資料庫頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1821">A database page containing index rows.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1822">索引檢視表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1822">indexed view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1823">套用了唯一叢集索引的檢視表，可改善某些查詢類型的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1823">A view with a unique clustered index applied on it to improve the performance of some types of queries.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1824">推斷攻擊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1824">inference attack</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1825">安全性威脅類型，其中惡意使用者能夠透過監視查詢的回應時間，推測出資料的值，而不需要實際存取資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1825">A type of security threat in which a malicious user is able to derive the value of data without actually accessing it, for example by monitoring the response time to a query.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1826">資訊模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1826">information model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1827">物件導向結構描述，它會定義用於指定應用程式、處理序、元件或軟體成品之結構和行為的中繼資料建構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1827">An object-oriented schema that defines metadata constructs used to specify the structure and behavior of an application, process, component, or software artifact.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1828">資訊技術</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1828">information technology</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1829">公司資料處理部門的正式名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1829">The formal name for a company's data processing department.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1830">初始快照集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1830">initial snapshot</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1831">包含複寫所需要之結構描述和資料、條件約束、擴充屬性、索引、觸發程序和系統資料表的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1831">Files that include schema and data, constraints, extended properties, indexes, triggers, and system tables that are necessary for replication.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1832">首次同步處理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1832">initial synchronization</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1833">指訂閱的第一次同步處理，在這期間會將複寫所需要的系統資料表和其他物件以及每個發行項的結構描述和資料複製到訂閱者端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1833">The first synchronization for a subscription, during which system tables and other objects that are required by replication, and the schema and data for each article, are copied to the Subscriber.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1834">初始磁帶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1834">initial tape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1835">在使用磁帶備份裝置的媒體集中，這是媒體家族中的第一個磁帶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1835">In a media set using tape backup devices, the first tape in a media family.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1836">inner join</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1836">inner join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1837">比較來源資料表所共用之資料行的值，以從多個來源資料表中擷取資料列的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1837">An operation that retrieves rows from multiple source tables by comparing the values from columns shared between the source tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1838">內部聯結會排除與其他來源資料表無相符資料列之來源資料表的資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1838">An inner join excludes rows from a source table that have no matching rows in the other source tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1839">親自驗證</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1839">in-person authentication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1840">完成憑證要求交易的實體驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1840">Physical authentication to complete a certificate request transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1841">例如，要求解除封鎖其個人識別碼 (PIN) 的使用者將會親自拜訪憑證管理員，以便提供包含身分識別的親自驗證，例如員工識別證或駕照。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1841">For example, an end user requesting his/her personal identification number (PIN) be unblocked will visit a certificate manager in person to provide in-person authentication with identification, such as an employee badge or drivers license.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1842">InProc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1842">InProc</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1843">從 DLL 檔案載入 COM 物件的程式碼，且與用戶端位於相同進程的情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1843">A circumstance where the COM object's code is loaded from a DLL file and is located in the same process as the client.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1844">輸入配接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1844">input adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1845">接受來自外部來源 (如資料庫、檔案、即時看板摘要、網路連接埠、製造裝置等) 之內送事件資料流的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1845">An adapter that accepts incoming event streams from external sources such as databases, files, ticker feeds, network ports, manufacturing devices and so on.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1846">輸入成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1846">input member</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1847">其值並非從其他資料計算得出，而是從資料來源中直接載入的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1847">A member whose value is loaded directly from the data source instead of being calculated from other data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1848">輸入集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1848">input set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1849">一組提供給多維度運算式 (MDX) 值運算式，由這個運算式來加以處理的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1849">The set of data provided to a Multidimensional Expressions (MDX) value expression upon which the expression operates.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1850">輸入來源</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1850">input source</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1851">用於做為查詢資訊來源的任何資料表、檢視表或結構描述圖解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1851">Any table, view, or schema diagram used as an information source for a query.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1852">輸入資料流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1852">input stream</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1853">在程式中當做與特定工作或目的地有關之一連串位元組使用的資訊流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1853">A flow of information used in a program as a sequence of bytes that are associated with a particular task or destination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1854">輸入資料流包括從鍵盤讀到記憶體中的一連串字元以及從磁碟檔案讀取的資料區塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1854">Input streams include series of characters read from the keyboard to memory and blocks of data read from disk files.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1855">非感應式資料指標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1855">insensitive cursor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1856">當資料指標開啟時，不反映其他使用者對於基礎資料之資料修改的資料指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1856">A cursor that does not reflect data modification made to the underlying data by other users while the cursor is open.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1857">插入事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1857">insert event</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1858">用於表示事件抵達資料流的事件種類。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1858">The event kind used to signify the arrival of an event into the stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1859">插入事件類型是由定義事件有效存留期間的中繼資料以及事件的裝載 (資料) 欄位所組成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1859">The insert event type consists of metadata that defines the valid lifetime of the event and the payload (data) fields of the event.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1860">插入查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1860">Insert Into query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1861">將一個資料表中的特定資料行和資料列複製到另一個資料表或相同資料表的查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1861">A query that copies specific columns and rows from one table to another or to the same table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1862">插入值查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1862">Insert Values query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1863">查詢 (SQL 陳述式)，它會建立新資料列，並將值插入至指定的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1863">A query (SQL statement) that creates a new row and inserts values into specified columns.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1864">instance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1864">instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1865">一個在電腦中執行的 SQL Server 複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1865">A copy of SQL Server running on a computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1866">執行個體控制提供者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1866">instance control provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1867">可讓您針對執行個體存放區中的工作流程執行個體發出控制命令的提供者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1867">A provider that allows you to issue control commands against workflow instances in an instance store.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1868">例如，SQL 控制提供者可讓您暫停、繼續或結束 SQL Server 資料庫中所儲存的執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1868">For example, a SQL control provider lets you suspend, resume, or terminate instances stored in a SQL Server database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1869">當您執行指令程式來控制執行個體存放區中的工作流程執行個體時，此指令程式會在內部針對該執行個體存放區使用控制提供者，以便傳送命令給執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1869">When you execute a cmdlet that controls a workflow instance in an instance store, the cmdlet internally uses the control provider for that instance store to send commands to the instance.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1870">執行個體查詢提供者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1870">instance query provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1871">可讓您針對執行個體存放區發出查詢的提供者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1871">A provider that allows you to issue queries against an instance store.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1872">例如，SQL 查詢提供者可讓您查詢 SQL Server 資料庫中所儲存的工作流程執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1872">For example, a SQL query provider lets you query for workflow instances stored in a SQL Server database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1873">當您執行指令程式來針對執行個體存放區查詢執行個體時，此指令程式會在內部使用查詢提供者，以便從該存放區擷取執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1873">When you execute a cmdlet that queries for instances against an instance store, the cmdlet internally uses the query provider to retrieve instances from that store.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1874">執行個體存放區</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1874">instance store</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1875">一組資料庫資料表，可儲存工作流程執行個體狀態和工作流程執行個體中繼資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1875">A set of database tables that store workflow instance state and workflow instance metadata.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1876">執行個體存放區提供者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1876">instance store provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1877">在 Windows AppFabric 中，可讓您建立執行個體存放區物件的提供者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1877">In Windows AppFabric, a provider that allows you to create instance store objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1878">例如，SQL 存放區提供者可讓用戶端建立 SQL 工作流程執行個體存放區物件，接著可讓用戶端將工作流程執行個體儲存到持續性存放區，以及從持續性存放區擷取工作流程執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1878">For example, a SQL store provider allows clients to create SQL workflow instance store objects, which in turn allows clients to save and retrieve workflow instances to and from a persistence store.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1879">整合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1879">integration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1880">在運算中，將不同的活動、程式或硬體元件結合成功能性單元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1880">In computing, the combining of different activities, programs, or hardware components into a functional unit.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1881">完整性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1881">integrity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1882">資料的精確度以及符合預期值的程度，特別是在傳送或處理之後。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1882">The accuracy of data and its conformity to its expected value, especially after being transmitted or processed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1883">完整性條件約束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1883">integrity constraint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1884">定義於資料表，用於防止會產生無效資料之資料修改的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1884">A property defined on a table that prevents data modifications that would create invalid data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1885">意圖鎖定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1885">intent lock</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1886">在資源階層的某一個層級上設定的鎖定，用於保護較低層級資源的共用或獨佔鎖定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1886">A lock that is placed on one level of a resource hierarchy to protect shared or exclusive locks on lower-level resources.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1887">意圖共用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1887">intent share</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1888">在資源階層的某一個層級上設定的鎖定，用於保護較低層級資源的共用或獨佔鎖定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1888">A lock that is placed on one level of a resource hierarchy to protect shared or exclusive locks on lower-level resources.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1889">互動式結構化查詢語言</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1889">interactive structured query language</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1890">SQL Server 所提供的互動式命令提示字元公用程式，可讓使用者從伺服器或工作站執行 Transact-SQL 陳述式或批次，以及檢視傳回的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1890">An interactive command prompt utility provided with SQL Server that lets users run Transact-SQL statements or batches from a server or workstation and view the results that are returned.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1891">interface</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1891">interface</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1892">一組形成行為和資料之邏輯分組的已定義屬性、方法和集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1892">A defined set of properties, methods, and collections that form a logical grouping of behaviors and data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1893">介面隱含式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1893">interface implication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1894">如果介面隱含另一個介面，任何實作第一個介面的類別也必須實作第二個介面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1894">If an interface implies another interface, then any class that implements the first interface must also implement the second interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1895">資訊模型利用介面隱含來得到某些多重繼承的效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1895">Interface implication is used in an information model to get some of the effects of multiple inheritance.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1896">中繼語言</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1896">intermediate language</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1897">當做原始來源語言 (通常是高階語言) 與目標語言 (通常是機器碼) 之間中繼步驟使用的電腦語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1897">A computer language used as an intermediate step between the original source language, usually a high-level language, and the target language, usually machine code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1898">某些高階編譯器會使用組合語言當做中繼語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1898">Some high-level compilers use assembly language as an intermediate language.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1899">國際電子電機委員會</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1899">International Electrotechnical Commission</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1900">負責開發國際資料通訊標準的兩個國際標準組織的其中之一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1900">One of two international standards bodies responsible for developing international data communications standards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1901">國際電子電機委員會 (IEC) 與國際標準組織 (ISO) 密切合作，共同定義運算的標準。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1901">The International Electrotechnical Commission (IEC) works closely with the International Organization for Standardization (ISO) to define standards of computing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1902">它們共同發行了 SQL 的 ISO/IEC SQL-92 標準。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1902">They jointly published the ISO/IEC SQL-92 standard for SQL.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1908">間隔事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1908">interval event</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1909">其裝載對於給定期間有效的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1909">An event whose payload is valid for a given period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1910">間隔事件的中繼資料需要在事件中繼資料中提供間隔的開始和結束時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1910">The metadata of the interval event requires that both the start and end time of the interval be provided in the event metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1911">間隔事件只有在這個特定間隔中才有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1911">Interval events are valid only for this specific interval.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1941">join</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1941">join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1942">結合兩份或更多資料表的內容，以及產生一個納入了各份資料表之資料列和資料行的結果集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1942">To combine the contents of two or more tables and produce a result set that incorporates rows and columns from each table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1943">聯結資料表時，通常會使用其共有的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1943">Tables are typically joined using data that they have in common.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1944">聯結資料行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1944">join column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1945">聯結條件所參考的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1945">A column referenced in a join condition.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1958">索引鍵</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1958">key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1959">識別快取中物件的字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1959">A string that identifies an object in the cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1960">這個字串在區域內必須是唯一的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1960">This string must be unique within a region.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1961">當加入物件然後使用索引鍵擷取時，物件便會與相同的索引鍵產生關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1961">Objects are associated with a key when they are added and then retrieved with the same key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1962">索引鍵</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1962">key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1963">在加密、驗證和數位簽章中，用來搭配演算法使用以加密或解密資訊的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1963">In encryption, authentication, and digital signatures, a value used in combination with an algorithm to encrypt or decrypt information.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1964">索引鍵</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1964">key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1965">在陣列中，組織及存取儲存的資料所依據的欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1965">In an array, the field by which stored data is organized and accessed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1966">索引鍵</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1966">key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1967">用於唯一識別資料列 (主索引鍵)、定義兩個資料表之間的關聯性 (外部索引鍵)，或是用於建立索引的資料行或資料行群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1967">A column or group of columns that uniquely identifies a row (primary key), defines the relationship between two tables (foreign key), or is used to build an index.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1974">關鍵效能指標 (key performance indicator)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1974">key performance indicator</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1975">預先定義的量值，用於追蹤策略性目標、目的、計劃、提議或商業流程的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1975">A predefined measure that is used to track performance of a strategic goal, objective, plan, initiative, or business process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1976">KPI 是針對目標進行評估。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1976">A KPI is evaluated against a target.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1977">從資料來源直接取得的明確且可測量的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1977">An explicit and measurable value taken directly from a data source.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1978">關鍵效能指標 (KPI) 是用來測量特定區域的效能，例如每位客戶的收入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1978">Key performance indicators (KPIs) are used to measure performance in a specific area, for example, revenue per customer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1979">關鍵範圍鎖定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1979">key range lock</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1980">用於鎖定資料表記錄之間的範圍，以防止對一組記錄新增或刪除虛設項目的鎖定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1980">A lock that is used to lock ranges between records in a table to prevent phantom additions to, or deletions from, a set of records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1981">這可以確保可序列化的交易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1981">Ensures serializable transactions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1982">金鑰修復</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1982">key recovery</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1983">復原使用者私密金鑰的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1983">The process of recovering a user's private key.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1987">索引鍵集驅動資料指標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1987">keyset-driven cursor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-1988">「在資料指標開啟時，會顯示其他使用者所進行的成員資料列更新效果，但不會顯示插入或刪除效果」的資料指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-1988">A cursor that shows the effects of updates made to its member rows by other users while the cursor is open, but does not show the effects of inserts or deletes.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2007">閂鎖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2007">latch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2008">短期同步處理物件，可保護不需要在交易週期內鎖定的動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2008">A short-term synchronization object protecting actions that need not be locked for the life of a transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2009">閂鎖主要用於保護儲存引擎積極地從基底資料表或索引傳送到關聯式引擎的資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2009">A latch is primarily used to protect a row that the storage engine is actively transferring from a base table or index to the relational engine.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2012">消極式載入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2012">lazy loading</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2013">資料載入模式，在此模式中除非存取導覽屬性，否則無法載入相關物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2013">A pattern of data loading where related objects are not loaded until a navigation property is accessed.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2032">左方外部聯結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2032">left outer join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2033">外部聯結類型，這種聯結類型會併入 JOIN 子句最左側資料表中的所有資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2033">A type of outer join in which all rows from the left-most table in the JOIN clause are included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2034">當左側資料表中的資料列不符合右側資料表中的資料列時，來自右側資料表的所有結果集資料行都會被指派 NULL 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2034">When rows in the left table are not matched by rows in the right table, all result set columns that come from the right table are assigned a value of NULL.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2035">等級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2035">level</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2036">維度階層中一組成員的名稱，這個組的所有成員與階層根的距離都相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2036">The name of a set of members in a dimension hierarchy such that all members of the set are at the same distance from the root of the hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2037">例如，時間階層可能包含年、月和日層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2037">For example, a time hierarchy may contain the levels Year, Month, and Day.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2040">輕量型共用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2040">lightweight pooling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2041">在對稱式多處理 (SMP) 環境中，有時候會出現內容切換過多的現象，這個選項藉由執行內容切換內嵌提供了減少這種現象對系統所造成額外負擔的方法，有助於減少使用者/核心的環狀轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2041">An option that provides a means of reducing the system overhead associated with the excessive context switching sometimes seen in symmetric multiprocessing (SMP) environments by performing the context switching inline, thus helping to reduce user/kernel ring transitions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2042">線條圖層 (line layer)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2042">line layer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2043">地圖報表中的圖層，會將空間資料顯示為表示路徑或路線的線條。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2043">The layer in a map report that displays spatial data as lines, for example, lines that indicate paths or routes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2044">連結維度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2044">linked dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2045">某個 Cube 中指向不同 Cube 之維度的參考 (也就是，Cube 中包含的不同資料來源檢視出現在相同或不同 Analysis Services 資料庫中)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2045">A reference in a cube to a dimension in a different cube (that is, a cube with a different data source view that exists in the same or a different Analysis Services database).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2046">連結的維度只能與來源 Cube 中的量值群組相關，而且只能在來源資料庫中進行編輯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2046">A linked dimension can only be related to measure groups in the source cube, and can only be edited in the source database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2047">連結量值群組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2047">linked measure group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2048">某個 Cube 中指向不同 Cube 之量值群組的參考 (也就是，Cube 中包含的不同資料來源檢視出現在相同或不同 Analysis Services 資料庫中)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2048">A reference in a cube to a measure group in a different cube (that is, a cube with a different data source view that exists in the same or a different Analysis Services database).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2049">連結量值群組只能在來源資料庫中編輯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2049">A linked measure group can only be edited in the source database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2050">連結的伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2050">linked server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2051">SQL Server 分散式查詢所使用的 OLE DB 資料來源定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2051">A definition of an OLE DB data source used by SQL Server distributed queries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2052">連結的伺服器定義指定存取資料時所需要的 OLE DB 提供者，其中包括 OLE DB 提供者足以連接資料的定址資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2052">The linked server definition specifies the OLE DB provider required to access the data, and includes enough addressing information for the OLE DB provider to connect to the data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2053">連結的資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2053">linked table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2054">OLE DB 資料列集。這是由已定義為連結的伺服器，且供 SQL Server 分散式查詢使用的 OLE DB 資料來源所公開。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2054">An OLE DB rowset exposed by an OLE DB data source that has been defined as a linked server for use in SQL Server distributed queries.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2055">連結資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2055">linking table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2056">與另外兩份資料表具有關聯的資料表，間接用於做為這兩份資料表之間的關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2056">A table that has associations with two other tables, and is used indirectly as an association between those two tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2057">LINQ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2057">LINQ</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2058">查詢語法，該語法會定義一組查詢運算子，允許使用任何 .NET 程式設計語言以直接宣告的方式表示周遊、篩選和投射作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2058">A query syntax that defines a set of query operators that allow traversal, filter, and projection operations to be expressed in a direct, declarative way in any .NET-based programming language.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2059">Little Endian</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2059">little endian</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2060">指的是採用先放置最不重要之位元組的方式來儲存數字的處理器記憶體架構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2060">Pertaining to a processor memory architecture that stores numbers so that the least significant byte is placed first.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2061">本機快取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2061">local cache</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2062">這項功能可讓還原序列化的快取物件複本儲存到執行具快取功能的應用程式之相同處理序的記憶體中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2062">A feature that enables deserialized copies of cached objects to be saved in the memory of the same process that runs the cache-enabled application.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2063">本機散發者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2063">local Distributor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2064">同時設定成 SQL Server 複寫的發行者和散發者的伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2064">A server that is configured as both a Publisher and a Distributor for SQL Server Replication.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2065">本機資料分割檢視</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2065">local partitioned view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2066">聯結單一伺服器中一組成員資料表之水平分割資料的檢視，讓資料看起來像是來自同一份資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2066">A view that joins horizontally partitioned data from a set of member tables across a single server, making the data appear as if from one table.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2069">地區設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2069">locale</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2070">某種語言與地理位置專屬的規則和資料集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2070">A collection of rules and data specific to a language and a geographic area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2071">地區設定包括有關排序規則、日期和時間格式、數值和貨幣慣例，以及字元分類的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2071">Locales include information on sorting rules, date and time formatting, numeric and monetary conventions, and character classification.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2072">當地語系化</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2072">localization</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2073">調整產品和/或內容 (包括文字和非文字元素) 以符合特定地區市場 (地區設定) 的語言、文化和政治期待和/或需求的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2073">The process of adapting a product and/or content (including text and non-text elements) to meet the language, cultural, and political expectations and/or requirements of a specific local market (locale).</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2076">鎖定擴大</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2076">lock escalation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2077">將許多細部鎖定轉換為較少廣泛鎖定的程序，藉此減少系統負擔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2077">The process of converting many fine-grain locks into fewer coarse-grain locks, thereby reducing system overhead.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2078">記錄備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2078">log backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2079">交易記錄的備份，其中包括先前的記錄備份中所未備份的所有記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2079">A backup of transaction logs that includes all log records not backed up in previous log backups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2080">記錄備份為完整和大量記錄復原模式下所需，但無法在簡單復原模式下使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2080">Log backups are required under the full and bulk-logged recovery models and are unavailable under the simple recovery model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2081">記錄鏈結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2081">log chain</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2082">資料庫交易記錄的連續順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2082">A continuous sequence of transaction logs for a database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2083">新記錄鏈結的開頭是建立資料庫之後，或資料庫從簡單復原模式切換到完整或大量記錄復原模式之後，所取出的第一個記錄備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2083">A new log chain begins with the first backup taken after the database is created, or when the database is switched from the simple to the full or bulk-logged recovery model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2084">在復原並還原之後，記錄鏈結就會分岔，以建立新的復原分支。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2084">A log chain forks after a restore followed by a recovery, creating a new recovery branch.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2085">記錄提供者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2085">log provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2086">在執行階段記錄封裝資訊的提供者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2086">A provider that logs package information at run time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2087">Integration Services 包含各種記錄提供者，因此能夠在封裝執行期間擷取事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2087">Integration Services includes a variety of log providers that make it possible to capture events during package execution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2088">記錄會以 XML、文字、資料庫或 Windows 事件記錄檔的格式建立和儲存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2088">Logs are created and stored in formats such as XML, text, database, or in the Windows event log.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2089">記錄讀取器代理程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2089">Log Reader Agent</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2090">在複寫中，負責監視針對異動複寫設定之每個資料庫的交易記錄，並將標示要複寫的交易從交易複製到散發資料庫中的可執行檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2090">In Replication, the executable that monitors the transaction of each database configured for transactional replication, and copies the transactions marked for replication from the transaction into the distribution database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2091">記錄序號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2091">log sequence number</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2092">在交易記錄中指派給每個項目的唯一號碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2092">A unique number assigned to each entry in a transaction log.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2093">LSN 會依據項目建立的順序指派。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2093">LSNs are assigned sequentially according to the order in which entries are created.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2094">記錄傳送</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2094">log shipping</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2095">定期將記錄備份從讀寫資料庫 (主要資料庫) 複製到一個或多個遠端伺服器執行個體 (次要伺服器)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2095">Copying, at regular intervals, log backup from a read-write database (the primary database) to one or more remote server instances (secondary servers).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2096">每一部次要伺服器都有一個稱為次要資料庫的唯讀資料庫，該資料庫是藉由還原主要資料庫的完整備份 (不含復原) 所建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2096">Each secondary server has a read-only database, called a secondary database, that was created by restoring a full backup of the primary database without recovery.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2097">次要伺服器會將每一個複製的記錄檔備份還原至次要資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2097">The secondary server restores each copied log backup to the secondary database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2098">次要伺服器為主要伺服器的暖待命伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2098">The secondary servers are warm standbys for the primary server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2099">記錄傳送設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2099">log shipping configuration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2100">一部主要伺服器、一部或多部次要伺服器 (各有一個次要資料庫) 以及一部監視伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2100">A single primary server, one or more secondary servers (each with a secondary database), and a monitor server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2101">記錄傳送作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2101">log shipping job</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2102">執行下列其中一項記錄傳送作業的作業：在主要伺服器上備份主要資料庫的交易記錄 (備份作業)、將交易記錄檔複製到次要伺服器 (複製作業)，或將記錄備份還原到次要伺服器上的次要資料庫 (還原作業)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2102">A job performing one of the following log-shipping operations: backing up the transaction log of the primary database at the primary server (the backup job), copying the transaction log file to a secondary server (the copy job), or restoring the log backup to the secondary database on a secondary server (the restore job).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2103">備份作業位於主要伺服器上；複製與還原作業則位於每一部次要伺服器上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2103">The backup job resides on the primary server; the copy and restore jobs reside on each of the secondary servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2104">請參閱：主要資料庫、主要伺服器、次要資料庫、次要伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2104">See also: primary database, primary server, secondary database, secondary server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2105">記錄接收</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2105">log sink</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2106">快取用戶端和快取主機的追蹤功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2106">A tracing function of the cache client and cache host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2107">記錄接收會從快取用戶端或快取主機擷取追蹤事件，並且可以在主控台中顯示這些事件、將事件寫入記錄檔，或是向 Windows 內的 Windows 事件追蹤 (ETW) 架構回報。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2107">Log sinks capture trace events from the cache client or cache host and can display them in a console, write them to a log file, or report them to the Event Tracing for Windows (ETW) framework inside Windows.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2108">邏輯錯誤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2108">logic error</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2109">像是錯誤的演算法這樣的錯誤，會造成程式產生不正確的結果，但不會阻止程式執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2109">An error, such as a faulty algorithm, that causes a program to produce incorrect results but does not prevent the program from running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2110">因此，邏輯錯誤經常不容易找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2110">Consequently, a logic error is often very difficult to find.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2111">邏輯名稱 (logical name)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2111">logical name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2112">SQL Server 用於識別檔案的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2112">A name used by SQL Server to identify a file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2113">邏輯記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2113">logical record</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2114">一項合併式複寫功能，可讓您定義不同資料表相關資料列之間的關聯性，以便將這些資料列當做一個單元來處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2114">A merge replication feature that allows you to define a relationship between related rows in different tables so that the rows are processed as a unit.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2115">登入識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2115">login ID</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2116">用來對作業系統、目錄服務或分散式系統識別使用者或實體的字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2116">A string that is used to identify a user or entity to an operating system, directory service, or distributed system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2117">例如，在 Windows® 整合式驗證中，登入名稱會使用 "DOMAIN\username" 格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2117">For example, in Windows® integrated authentication, a login name uses the form "DOMAIN\username."</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2118">登入安全性模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2118">login security mode</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2119">這種安全性模式會決定 SQL Server 執行個體驗證登入要求的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2119">A security mode that determines the manner in which an instance of SQL Server validates a login request.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2120">完整剖析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2120">long parsing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2121">在 SQL 系統中，有兩種典型的執行緒：短執行緒是短時間使用資源的處理序，長執行緒則是長時間使用資源的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2121">In the SQL system there are two typical types of threads: - short thread: it is a process that use the resources for a short time and - long thread: it is a process that use the resources for a long time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2122">完整剖析是針對長時間存在的執行緒所進行的分析。注意：長/短的定義是根據每一個處理序的系統計算/統計資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2122">long parsing: is the analysis of the threads that lived for a long time Note: the definition of short/long is based on the system calculation/statistic for each process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2123">最低盒值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2123">Low Box</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2124">盒狀圖上的最低盒值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2124">The lowest value of a box on a Box Plot chart.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2125">下限標準</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2125">low watermark</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2126">每一部快取主機上的記憶體耗用量臨界值，指定過期的物件從記憶體中收回的時機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2126">A memory consumption threshold on each cache host that specifies when expired objects are evicted out of memory.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2127">最低鬚值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2127">low whisker</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2128">盒狀圖上不是極端值的最低值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2128">The lowest value that is not an outlier on a box plot chart.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2129">LRU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2129">LRU</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2130">快取叢集使用的收回類型，其中最少用的物件會在最常用的物件之前收回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2130">The type of eviction used by the cache cluster, where least recently used objects are evicted before the most recently used objects.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2131">LSN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2131">LSN</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2132">在交易記錄中指派給每個項目的唯一號碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2132">A unique number assigned to each entry in a transaction log.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2133">LSN 會依據項目建立的順序指派。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2133">LSNs are assigned sequentially according to the order in which entries are created.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2134">引誘攻擊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2134">luring attack</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2135">引誘用戶端自願連接到攻擊者的攻擊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2135">An attack in which the client is lured to voluntarily connect to the attacker.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2136">建立方式知識</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2136">made-with knowledge</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2137">在同步處理程序中，用於衝突偵測的最新來源複本知識。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2137">In synchronization processes, the current knowledge of the source replica, to be used in conflict detection.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2138">管理關聯性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2138">Manage Relationships</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2139">UI 項目，可讓使用者在模型中檢視、刪除或建立新的關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2139">A UI element that enables a user to view, delete or create new relationships in a model.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2155">多對多維度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2155">many-to-many dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2156">維度與量值群組之間的關聯性，其中單一事實可能會與許多維度成員產生關聯，而單一維度成員可能會與許多事實產生關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2156">A relationship between a dimension and a measure group in which a single fact may be associated with many dimension members and a single dimension member may be associated with a many facts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2157">為了定義維度和事實資料表之間的這項關聯性，維度會加入至中繼事實資料表，接著中繼事實資料表就會加入至加入事實資料表的中繼維度資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2157">To define this relationship between the dimension and the fact table, the dimension is joined to an intermediate fact table and the intermediate fact table is joined, in turn, to an intermediate dimension table that is joined to the fact table.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2214">矩陣資料區域 (matrix data region)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2214">matrix data region</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2215">這是在報表配置中以變數分欄格式顯示資料的報表項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2215">A report item on a report layout that displays data in a variable columnar format.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2216">MBCS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2216">MBCS</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2217">這是混合寬度的字元集，其中某些字元是由 1 個以上的位元組所組成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2217">A mixed-width character set, in which some characters consist of more than 1 byte.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2218">MBCS 會用於日文、中文和韓文等語言，因為單一位元組字元集的 256 個值不足以表示這些語言中所有可能的字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2218">An MBCS is used in languages such as Japanese, Chinese, and Korean, where the 256 possible values of a single-byte character set are not sufficient to represent all possible characters.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2229">媒體家族</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2229">media family</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2230">備份作業寫入媒體集所使用之備份裝置的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2230">Data written by a backup operation to a backup device used by a media set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2231">在只有單一裝置的媒體集中，只會有一個媒體家族存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2231">In a media set with only a single device, only one media family exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2232">在等量媒體集中，則會有多個媒體家族存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2232">In a striped media set, multiple media families exist.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2233">如果等量媒體集並無鏡像，則每一個裝置都會對應到一個家族。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2233">If the striped media set is unmirrored, each device corresponds to a family.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2234">鏡像的媒體集包含每個媒體家族的兩到四個相同副本 (稱為鏡像)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2234">A mirrored media set contains from two to four identical copies of each media family (called mirrors).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2235">將備份附加至媒體集會使其媒體家族擴大。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2235">Appending backups to a media set extends its media families.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2240">中位數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2240">median</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2241">排序的數字集合中的中間值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2241">The middle value in a set of ordered numbers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2242">藉由在集合中選擇至少有一半的值小於選擇的最小值，來決定中間值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2242">The median value is determined by choosing the smallest value such that at least half of the values in the set are no greater than the chosen value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2243">如果集合內值的數目是奇數，則中間值對應至單一的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2243">If the number of values within the set is odd, the median value corresponds to a single value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2244">如果集合內值的數目是偶數，則中間值對應至兩個中間值的總和除以 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2244">If the number of values within the set is even, the median value corresponds to the sum of the two middle values divided by two.</span></span>|
