|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2344">鏡像伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2344">mirror server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2345">在資料庫鏡像組態中，指鏡像資料庫所在的伺服器執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2345">In a database mirroring configuration, the server instance where the mirror database resides.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2346">鏡像伺服器是鏡像夥伴，其資料庫副本目前是鏡像資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2346">The mirror server is the mirroring partner whose copy of the database is currently the mirror database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2347">鏡像伺服器是熱待命伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2347">The mirror server is a hot standby server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2348">鏡像媒體集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2348">mirrored media set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2349">包含每個媒體家族中兩到四個相同副本 (鏡像) 的媒體集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2349">A media set that contains two to four identical copies (mirrors) of each media family.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2350">還原作業只需要每個系列一個鏡像，讓鏡像的對應磁碟區能夠取代損毀的媒體磁碟區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2350">Restore operations require only one mirror per family, allowing a damaged media volume to be replaced by the corresponding volume from a mirror.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2351">鏡像</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2351">mirroring</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2352">這項程序會立即將讀取/寫入資料庫 (主體資料庫) 的每項更新重製到 Database Engine 個別執行個體 (鏡像伺服器) 上的資料庫唯讀鏡像 (鏡像資料庫)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2352">Immediately reproducing every update to a read-write database (the principal database) onto a read-only mirror of that database (the mirror database) residing on a separate instance of the database engine (the mirror server).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2353">在實際執行環境中，鏡像伺服器位於另一部電腦上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2353">In production environments, the mirror server is on another machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2354">鏡像資料庫是在不復原的情況下，藉由還原主體資料庫的完整備份所建立的一種資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2354">The mirror database is created by restoring a full backup of the principal database (without recovery).</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2360">模數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2360">modulo</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2361">一項算術運算，其結果是除法運算的餘數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2361">An arithmetic operation whose result is the remainder of a division operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2362">例如，17 modulo 3 = 2，因為 17 除以 3 會得出餘數 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2362">For example, 17 modulo 3 = 2 because 17 divided by 3 yields a remainder of 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2363">模數運算是在程式設計中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2363">Modulo operations are used in programming.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2364">「監視伺服器」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2364">monitor server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2365">在記錄傳送設定中，這個伺服器執行個體的歷程和狀態會由每項記錄傳送作業進行記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2365">In a log shipping configuration, a server instance on which every log shipping job in the configuration records its history and status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2366">每一個記錄傳送組態都有自己專用的監視伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2366">Each log shipping configuration has its own dedicated monitor server.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2390">多使用者 (multiuser)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2390">multiuser</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2391">與可由多人使用的任何電腦系統有關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2391">Pertaining to any computer system that can be used by more than one person.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2392">雖然多人共用的微電腦可以視為多使用者系統，但是這個詞彙通常專指可由多人透過通訊設備或經由網路終端機同步存取的機器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2392">Although a microcomputer shared by several people can be considered a multiuser system, the term is generally reserved for machines that can be accessed simultaneously by several people through communications facilities or via network terminals.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2393">mutex</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2393">mutex</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2394">一項程式設計技術，可確保一次只有一個程式或常式能夠存取某些資源，例如記憶體位置、I/O 連接埠或檔案，通常存取的方式是使用信號，這些信號是在程式中用來協調多個程式或常式之活動的旗標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2394">A programming technique that ensures that only one program or routine at a time can access some resource, such as a memory location, an I/O port, or a file, often through the use of semaphores, which are flags used in programs to coordinate the activities of more than one program or routine.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2445">非自主資料庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2445">non-contained database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2446">將資料庫設定和中繼資料儲存在資料庫安裝所在 SQL Server Database Engine 執行個體中的 SQL Server 資料庫，且該資料庫會要求登入 master 資料庫進行驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2446">A SQL Server database that stores database settings and metadata with the instance of SQL Server Database Engine where the database is installed, and requires logins in the master database for authentication.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2447">非索引鍵之索引資料行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2447">Nonkey index column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2448">在非叢集索引中，並未當做索引鍵資料行參與的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2448">Column in a nonclustered index that does not participate as a key column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2449">不過，此資料行會儲存在索引的分頁層級而且與索引鍵資料行一起用於涵蓋一個或多個查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2449">Rather, the column is stored in the leaf-level of the index and is used in conjunction with the key columns to cover one or more queries.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2471">Null 指標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2471">null pointer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2472">未指向任何目標的指標：通常是標準化的記憶體位址，例如 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2472">A pointer to nothing: usually a standardized memory address, such as 0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2473">null 指標通常標記線性指標序列的最後一個，或是表示資料搜尋作業結果是空的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2473">A null pointer usually marks the last of a linear sequence of pointers or indicates that a data search operation has come up empty.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2474">Null 屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2474">nullability</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2475">資料行、參數或變數用於指定是否接受 null 資料值的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2475">The attribute of a column, parameter, or variable that specifies whether it allows null data values.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2476">允許為 NULL 屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2476">nullable property</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2477">控制某個欄位是否可以有 NULL 值的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2477">A property which controls if a field can have a NULL value.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2478">NUMA 節點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2478">NUMA node</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2479">有自己的記憶體，且可能的話，也有自己的 I/O 通道的處理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2479">A group of processors with its own memory and possibly its own I/O channels.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2480">數值陣列</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2480">numeric array</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2481">由索引鍵集合和值集合所組成的陣列，其中每一個索引鍵都與一個值有關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2481">An array composed of a collection of keys and a collection of values, where each key is associated with one value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2482">值可以是任何類型，但索引鍵必須是數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2482">The values can be of any type, but the keys must be numeric.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2483">數值運算式 (numeric expression)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2483">numeric expression</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2484">會評估得出數字的任何運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2484">Any expression that evaluates to a number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2485">運算式可以是任何包含變數、常數、函數和運算子的組合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2485">The expression can be any combination of variables, constants, functions, and operators.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2486">物件識別碼 (object identifier)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2486">object identifier</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2487">識別物件類別或屬性的數字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2487">A number that identifies an object class or attribute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2488">物件識別碼 (OID) 會依據業界通用的階層進行編排。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2488">Object identifiers (OIDs) are organized into an industry-wide global hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2489">物件識別碼會以含有點的十進位字串表示，例如 1.2.3.4，其中每一個點代表階層中的新分支。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2489">An object identifier is represented as a dotted decimal string, such as 1.2.3.4, with each dot representing a new branch in the hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2490">國家/地區註冊授權單位會向個人或組織發出根物件識別項，這些個人或組織會管理其根物件識別項之下的階層。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2490">National/regional registration authorities issue root object identifiers to individuals or organizations, who manage the hierarchy below their root object identifier.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2491">物件存留期</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2491">object lifetime</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2492">快取的物件位於快取中，並且可供快取用戶端擷取的時間長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2492">The span of time a cached object resides in cache and is available to be retrieved by cache clients.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2493">存留期結束時，物件就會過期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2493">The object expires when its lifetime ends.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2494">過期的物件無法供快取用戶端擷取，但是會持續保留在快取主機的記憶體中，直到收回為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2494">Expired objects cannot be retrieved by cache clients, but remain in memory of the cache host until they are evicted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2495">也稱為存留時間 (TTL)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2495">Specified as time to live (TTL).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2496">物件變數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2496">object variable</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2497">包含對物件之參考的變數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2497">A variable that contains a reference to an object.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2498">ODS 程式庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2498">ODS library</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2499">C 函數集，可讓應用程式成為伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2499">A set of C functions that makes an application a server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2500">ODS 程式庫呼叫會回應用戶端/伺服器網路中，來自用戶端的要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2500">ODS library calls respond to requests from a client in a client/server network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2501">此外還會管理用戶端和伺服器之間的通訊和資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2501">Also manages the communication and data between the client and the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2502">ODS 程式庫遵循表格式資料流 (TDS) 通訊協定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2502">ODS library follows the tabular data stream (TDS) protocol.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2503">Office 檔案驗證</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2503">Office File Validation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2504">一項安全功能，此功能會先驗證檔案，才允許應用程式載入檔案，藉此防堵檔案格式漏洞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2504">A security feature that validates files before allowing them to be loaded by the application, in order to protect against file format vulnerabilities.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2505">離線還原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2505">offline restore</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2506">在資料庫離線的狀態下進行的還原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2506">A restore during which the database is offline.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2507">OLAP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2507">OLAP</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2508">利用多維度結構來提供資料的快速存取以進行分析的技術。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2508">A technology that uses multidimensional structures to provide rapid access to data for analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2509">OLAP 的來源資料通常儲存在關聯式資料庫的資料倉儲中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2509">The source data for OLAP is commonly stored in data warehouses in a relational database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2510">OLAP Cube</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2510">OLAP cube</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2511">一組資料，可組織和摘要成一組由維度或量值所定義的多維度結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2511">A set of data that is organized and summarized into a multidimensional structure that is defined by a set of dimensions and measures.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2512">OLAP 資料庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2512">OLAP database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2513">關聯式資料庫系統，透過多維度存取資料 (以數種不同準則檢視資料)、大量計算能力及專門的索引技術，能夠處理的查詢比標準關聯式資料庫所處理的查詢更為複雜。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2513">A relational database system capable of handling queries more complex than those handled by standard relational databases, through multidimensional access to data (viewing the data by several different criteria), intensive calculation capability, and specialized indexing techniques.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2514">一次密碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2514">one-time password</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2515">由特殊密碼產生軟體或硬體 Token 所產生，而且只能使用一次的密碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2515">Passwords produced by special password generating software or by a hardware token and that can be used only once.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2516">線上分析處理 (online analytical processing)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2516">online analytical processing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2517">利用多維度結構來提供資料的快速存取以進行分析的技術。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2517">A technology that uses multidimensional structures to provide rapid access to data for analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2518">OLAP 的來源資料通常儲存在關聯式資料庫的資料倉儲中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2518">The source data for OLAP is commonly stored in data warehouses in a relational database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2519">線上還原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2519">online restore</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2520">指當資料庫維持在線上時，還原一個或多個次要檔案群組、屬於次要檔案群組的檔案或頁面的還原作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2520">A restore in which one or more secondary filegroups, files belonging to secondary filegroups, or pages are restored while the database remains online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2521">線上還原僅適用於 SQL Server 2005 Enterprise Edition (包括 Evaluation 和 Developer Edition)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2521">Online restore is available only in the SQL Server 2005 Enterprise Edition (including the Evaluation and Developer Editions).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2522">開放式資料服務程式庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2522">Open Data Services library</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2523">C 函數集，可讓應用程式成為伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2523">A set of C functions that makes an application a server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2524">ODS 程式庫呼叫會回應用戶端/伺服器網路中，來自用戶端的要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2524">ODS library calls respond to requests from a client in a client/server network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2525">此外還會管理用戶端和伺服器之間的通訊和資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2525">Also manages the communication and data between the client and the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2526">ODS 程式庫遵循表格式資料流 (TDS) 通訊協定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2526">ODS library follows the tabular data stream (TDS) protocol.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2527">作業碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2527">operation code</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2528">機器語言或組合語言指令的一部分，會指定指令的類型與其作用所在的資料結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2528">The portion of a machine language or assembly language instruction that specifies the type of instruction and the structure of the data on which it operates.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2529">! 運算子之後</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2529">operator</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2530">查詢的原子單位 (Atomic Unit)，由 StreamInsight 伺服器排程以處理套用查詢的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2530">An atomic unit of a query as scheduled by the StreamInsight server to process the events on which the query is applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2531">範例包括 SELECT、PROJECT、AGGREGATE、UNION、TOP K 和 JOIN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2531">Examples include SELECT, PROJECT, AGGREGATE, UNION, TOP K and JOIN.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2532">運算子是完全可組合的，而且具有特定的輸入和輸出數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2532">Operators are fully composable and have a specific number of inputs and outputs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2533">請參閱其他詞彙：查詢、查詢範本、可組合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2533">See Other Terms: query, query template, composable.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2534">! 運算子之後</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2534">operator</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2535">指定要在運算式內執行之計算類型的符號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2535">A sign or symbol that specifies the type of calculation to perform within an expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2536">目前有數學、比較、邏輯和參考運算子。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2536">There are mathematical, comparison, logical, and reference operators.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2537">開放式並行存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2537">optimistic concurrency</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2538">使用快取物件的版本資訊管理並行存取的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2538">A method of managing concurrency by using a cached object's version information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2539">由於每次物件更新都會改變其版本號碼，因此使用版本資訊可避免更新覆寫其他人的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2539">Because every update to an object changes its version number, using version information prevents the update from overwriting someone else's changes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2540">最佳化同步處理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2540">optimize synchronization</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2541">合併式複寫中的選項，可讓您在判斷最近的變更是否造成某個資料列移入或移出發行至訂閱者的資料分割時，將網路流量降至最低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2541">An option in merge replication that allows you to minimize network traffic when determining whether recent changes have caused a row to move into or out of a partition that is published to a Subscriber.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2542">已排序集合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2542">ordered set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2543">依特定順序傳回的一組成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2543">A set of members returned in a specific order.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2546">OTP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2546">OTP</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2547">由特殊密碼產生軟體或硬體 Token 所產生，而且只能使用一次的密碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2547">Passwords produced by special password generating software or by a hardware token and that can be used only once.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2548">outer join</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2548">outer join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2549">將符合搜尋條件之聯結資料表的所有資料列包括在內的聯結，即使一個資料表在其他聯結資料表中沒有相符的資料列，它的資料列也會包括在內。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2549">A join that includes all the rows from the joined tables that meet the search conditions, even rows from one table for which there is no matching row in the other join table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2550">輸出配接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2550">output adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2551">接收伺服器所處理的事件、將事件轉換成輸出裝置所預期的格式 (資料庫、文字檔、PDA 或其他裝置)，並將資料發出到該裝置的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2551">An adapter that receives events processed by the server, transforms the events into a format expected by the output device (a database, text file, PDA, or other device), and emits the data to that device.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2552">輸出資料行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2552">output column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2553">在 SQL Server Integration Services 中，是指來源會將其加入至資料流程，並且可做為輸入資料行加入至資料流程中下一個資料流程元件的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2553">In SQL Server Integration Services, a column that the source adds to the data flow and that is available as input column to the next data flow component in the data flow.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2554">輸出資料流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2554">output stream</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2555">離開電腦系統，而且與特定工作或目的地相關聯的資訊流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2555">A flow of information that leaves a computer system and is associated with a particular task or destination.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2556">過度學習</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2556">overfitting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2557">資料中的隨機變數誤分類為重要模式時，資料採礦中發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2557">A problem in data mining when random variations in data are misclassified as important patterns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2558">過度學習經常在資料集太小，無法代表真實情況時發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2558">Overfitting often occurs when the data set is too small to represent the real world.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2559">擁有權鏈結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2559">ownership chain</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2560">指當一個物件參考其他物件，而發出呼叫與被呼叫的物件由相同使用者擁有時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2560">When an object references other objects and the calling and the called objects are owned by the same user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2561">SQL Server 會使用擁有權鏈結決定如何檢查權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2561">SQL Server uses the ownership chain to determine how to check permissions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2562">套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2562">package</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2563">當做一個單位執行之控制流程與資料流程元素的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2563">A collection of control flow and data flow elements that runs as a unit.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2564">封包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2564">packet</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2565">在網路上從某一部電腦或裝置傳輸到另一部的資訊單位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2565">A unit of information transmitted from one computer or device to another on a network.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2566">索引頁預留空間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2566">Pad index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2567">這個選項可指定在索引的中繼層級中，每一頁上要保留的空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2567">An option that specifies the space to leave open on each page in the intermediate levels of the index.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2568">填補 (padding)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2568">padding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2569">在資料儲存中，這項動作會將一個或多個位元 (通常是零) 加入至資料區塊中以便填滿該區塊、強制實際資料位元進入特定位置，或是避免資料複製已有既定意義的位元模式 (例如內嵌命令)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2569">In data storage, the addition of one or more bits, usually zeros, to a block of data in order to fill it, to force the actual data bits into a certain position, or to prevent the data from duplicating a bit pattern that has an established meaning, such as an embedded command</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2570">頁面</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2570">page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2571">以較小資料子集傳回查詢結果，讓使用者能夠藉由檢視「多頁」資料導覽結果集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2571">To return the results of a query in smaller subsets of data, thus making it possible for the user to navigate through the result set by viewing 'pages' of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2572">頁面</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2572">page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2573">在虛擬儲存體系統中，這是固定長度的連續虛擬位址區塊，在分頁作業期間，這個區塊會做為一個單元而在記憶體和磁碟之間來回複製。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2573">In a virtual storage system, a fixed-length block of contiguous virtual addresses copied as a unit from memory to disk and back during paging operations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2574">分頁錯誤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2574">page fault</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2575">當軟體嘗試從標記為「不存在」的虛擬記憶體位置讀取或寫入其中時發生的中斷情形。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2575">The interrupt that occurs when software attempts to read from or write to a virtual memory location that is marked "not present."</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2576">分頁還原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2576">page restore</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2577">還原一個或多個資料頁的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2577">An operation that restores one or more data pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2578">分頁還原主要是修復隔離的損毀頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2578">Page restore is intended for repairing isolated damaged pages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2579">pager</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2579">pager</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2580">口袋大小的無線電子裝置，會使用無線電訊號記錄來電號碼或簡訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2580">A pocket-sized wireless electronic device that uses radio signals to record incoming phone numbers or short text messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2581">某些呼叫器還可讓使用者傳送訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2581">Some pagers allow users to send messages as well.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2582">呼叫系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2582">paging system</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2583">可讓使用者在範圍外時傳送和接收訊息的系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2583">A system that allows users to send and receive messages when they are out of range.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2584">PAL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2584">PAL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2585">保護發行者安全的主要機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2585">The primary mechanism for securing the Publisher.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2586">它包含已授與發行集之存取權的登入、帳戶與群組清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2586">It contains a list of logins, accounts, and groups that are granted access to the publication.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2587">平行執行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2587">parallel execution</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2588">明顯同步執行兩個或多個常式或程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2588">The apparently simultaneous execution of two or more routines or programs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2589">並行執行可以在單一處理序上或使用時間共用技術達成，例如將程式分成不同的執行工作或執行緒，或是使用多個處理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2589">Concurrent execution can be accomplished on a single process or by using time-sharing techniques, such as dividing programs into different tasks or threads of execution, or by using multiple processors.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2590">平行處理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2590">parallel processing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2591">處理方法，只能在同步執行兩個或多個處理器的電腦上執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2591">A method of processing that can run only on a computer that contains two or more processors running simultaneously.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2592">平行處理與多重處理的差異在於，前者的工作會分散至可用的處理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2592">Parallel processing differs from multiprocessing in the way a task is distributed over the available processors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2593">在多重處理中，處理序可能會分成序列區塊，其中某一個處理器管理資料庫存取、第二個分析資料，而第三個處理畫面的圖形輸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2593">In multiprocessing, a process might be divided up into sequential blocks, with one processor managing access to a database, another analyzing the data, and a third handling graphical output to the screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2594">程式設計師若採用執行平行處理的系統，則必須找出劃分工作的方式，將該工作大致平均分配給可用的處理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2594">Programmers working with systems that perform parallel processing must find ways to divide a task so that it is more or less evenly distributed among the processors available.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2595">參數化查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2595">parameterized query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2596">接受以參數做為輸入值的查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2596">A query that accepts input values through parameters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2597">參數化報表 (parameterized report)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2597">parameterized report</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2598">已發行的報表，可透過參數接受輸入值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2598">A published report that accepts input values through parameters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2599">參數化資料列篩選器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2599">parameterized row filter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2600">合併式複寫所能使用的資料列篩選器，它可讓您依據系統函數或使用者定義函數 (例如：SUSER_SNAME()) 來限制複寫到訂閱者的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2600">A row filter available with merge replication that allows you to restrict the data replicated to a Subscriber based on a system function or user-defined function (for example: SUSER_SNAME()).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2601">部分備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2601">partial backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2602">主要檔案群組、每個讀取-寫入檔案群組以及任何選擇性指定之檔案中所有資料的備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2602">A backup of all the data in the primary filegroup, every read-write filegroup, and any optionally specified files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2603">唯讀資料庫的部分備份只包含主要檔案群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2603">A partial backup of a read-only database contains only the primary filegroup.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2604">部分資料庫還原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2604">partial database restore</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2605">只包含一部分資料庫的還原，包括其主要檔案群組，以及一個或多個次要檔案群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2605">A restore of only a portion of a database consisting of its primary filegroup and one or more secondary filegroups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2606">其他檔案群組會永遠保持離線狀態，不過之後可以將其還原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2606">The other filegroups remain permanently offline, though they can be restored later.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2607">部分差異備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2607">partial differential backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2608">相對於先前的單一部分備份 (基底備份) 而言，差異的部分備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2608">A partial backup that is differential relative to a single, previous partial backup (the base backup).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2609">若為唯讀資料庫，則是指只包含主要檔案群組的部分差異備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2609">For a read-only database, a partial differential backup contains only the primary filegroup.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2610">參與者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2610">participant</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2611">同步處理提供者及其關聯的複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2611">A synchronization provider and its associated replica.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2612">小品詞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2612">particle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2613">非常小的片段或部分，而且它是不可分割的物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2613">A very small piece or part; an indivisible object.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2614">資料分割函數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2614">partition function</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2615">定義資料分割資料表或索引的資料列如何依據特定資料行 (稱為分割資料行) 的值分散到資料分割集的函數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2615">A  function that defines how the rows of a partitioned table or index are spread across a set of partitions based on the values of certain columns, called partitioning columns.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2616">資料分割配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2616">partition scheme</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2617">將分割區函數的資料分割對應至一組檔案群組的資料庫物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2617">A database object that maps the partitions of a partition function to a set of filegroups.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2618">資料分割索引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2618">partitioned index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2619">在資料分割配置上建立的索引，它的資料水平分成若干單元，且這些單元可能散佈在資料庫的多個檔案群組中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2619">An index built on a partition scheme, and whose data is horizontally divided into units which may be spread across more than one filegroup in a database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2620">分割快照集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2620">partitioned snapshot</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2621">在合併式複寫中，只包含單一資料分割之資料的快照集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2621">In merge replication, a snapshot that includes only the data from a single partition.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2622">資料分割資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2622">partitioned table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2623">在資料分割配置上建立的資料表，它的資料水平分成若干單元，且這些單元可能散佈在資料庫的多個檔案群組中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2623">A table built on a partition scheme, and whose data is horizontally divided into units which may be spread across more than one filegroup in a database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2624">分割資料表平行處理原則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2624">partitioned table parallelism</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2625">適用於從資料分割物件選取之查詢的平行執行策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2625">The parallel execution strategy for queries that select from partitioned objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2626">在執行策略中，查詢處理器會判斷查詢所需的資料表資料分割，以及配置給每一個資料分割的執行緒比例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2626">As part of the execution strategy, the query processor determines the table partitions that are required for the query and the proportion of threads to allocate to each partition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2627">在大多數情況下，查詢處理器會將相同或幾乎相同的執行緒數目配置給每一個資料分割，然後以平行方式在資料分割之間執行查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2627">In most cases, the query processor allocates an equal or almost equal number of threads to each partition, and then executes the query in parallel across the partitions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2628">分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2628">partitioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2629">用多個較小型的資料表來取代單一資料表的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2629">The process of replacing a table with multiple smaller tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2630">分割資料行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2630">partitioning column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2631">資料分割函數用於分割資料表或索引的資料表或索引資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2631">The column of a table or index that a partition function uses to partition a table or index.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2632">夥伴</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2632">partner</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2633">指資料庫鏡像中的主體伺服器或鏡像伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2633">In database mirroring, refers to the principal server or the mirror server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2634">行程順序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2634">pass order</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2635">多維度 Cube 中導出成員、自訂成員、自訂積存公式及計算資料格的評估順序 (從最高到最低的計算行程號碼) 和計算順序 (從最低到最高的計算行程號碼)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2635">The order of evaluation (from highest to lowest calculation pass number) and calculation (from lowest to highest calculation pass number) for calculated members, custom members, custom rollup formulas, and calculated cells in a multidimensional cube.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2636">複雜密碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2636">pass phrase</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2637">用來取得網路、程式或資料之存取權的一連串字詞或其他文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2637">A sequence of words or other text used to gain access to a network, program, or data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2638">為了提高安全性，複雜密碼通常會比較長。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2638">A passphrase is generally longer for added security.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2639">傳遞查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2639">pass-through query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2640">SQL 專用的查詢，用於直接將命令傳送至 ODBC 資料庫伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2640">An SQL-specific query you use to send commands directly to an ODBC database server.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2652">點對點複寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2652">peer-to-peer replication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2653">異動複寫的類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2653">A type of transactional replication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2654">與唯讀異動複寫和使用更新訂閱的異動複寫相反，點對點複寫拓撲中各節點之間的關聯性是對等的關聯性，而不是階層式關聯性，其中每個節點都包含相同的結構描述和資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2654">In contrast to read-only transactional replication and transactional replication with updating subscriptions, the relationships between nodes in a Peer to Peer replication topology are peer relationships rather than hierarchical ones, with each node containing identical schema and data.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2718">時間點事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2718">point event</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2719">在單一時間點所發生的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2719">An event occurrence as of a single point in time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2720">只需要事件的開始時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2720">Only the start time is required for the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2721">CEP 伺服器會推斷有效的結束時間，其方式是將刻度 (基礎時間資料類型的最小時間單位) 加入到開始時間，以設定事件的有效時間間隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2721">The CEP server infers the valid end time by adding a tick (the smallest unit of time in the underlying time data type) to the start time to set the valid time interval for the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2722">時間點事件只有在這個單一時間才有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2722">Point events are valid only for this single instant of time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2723">時間點事件模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2723">point event model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2724">時間點事件的事件模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2724">The event model of a point event.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2725">點圖層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2725">point layer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2726">地圖報表中的圖層，會將空間資料 (例如城市或有趣的景點) 顯示為不同的點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2726">The layer in a map report that displays spatial data as points, for examples, points that indicate cities or points of interest.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2727">指標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2727">pointer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2728">指針、標記或橫條，指出以報表上的刻度顯示的單一值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2728">A needle, marker, or bar that indicates a single value displayed against a scale on a report.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2729">時間點復原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2729">point-in-time recovery</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2730">只復原記錄備份內在特定時間點之前已認可之交易的程序，而不是復原整個備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2730">The process of recovering only the transactions within a log backup that were committed before a specific point in time, instead of recovering the whole backup.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2731">有害訊息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2731">poison message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2732">包含應用程式無法成功處理之資訊的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2732">A message containing information that an application cannot successfully process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2733">有害訊息不是損毀的訊息，也可能不是無效要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2733">A poison message is not a corrupt message, and may not be an invalid request.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2734">原則模組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2734">policy module</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2735">這項憑證服務元件可決定應該自動核准、拒絕憑證要求，或將其標記為暫止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2735">A Certificate Services component that determines whether a certificate request should be automatically approved, denied, or marked as pending.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2736">原則式管理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2736">policy-based management</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2737">一組內建函數，會針對 SQL Server 中的值、物件和設定傳回相關的伺服器狀態資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2737">A set of built-in functions that return server state information about values, objects, and settings in SQL Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2738">原則式管理可讓資料庫管理員宣告所要的系統狀態，並且檢查系統是否符合該狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2738">Policy Based Management allows a database administrator to declare the desired state of the system and checks the system for compliance with that state.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2739">輪詢者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2739">poller</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2740">監視其他元件之狀態的元件或介面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2740">A component or interface that monitors the status of other components.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2741">它會藉由重覆輪詢其他元件以提供目前狀態的方式執行其功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2741">It performs this function by repeatedly polling the other component to provide its current status.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2742">輪詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2742">polling</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2743">定期判斷集合中每個裝置之狀態的程序，讓作用中程式能夠處理每個裝置產生的事件，例如滑鼠按鈕是否為按下狀態，或序列連接埠上是否有可用的新資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2743">The process of periodically determining the status of each device in a set so that the active program can process the events generated by each device, such as whether a mouse button was pressed or whether new data is available at a serial port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2744">與此程序相對的就是事件驅動的處理，其中作業系統會藉由中斷或訊息警示程式或常式有事件發生，而不必輪流檢查每個裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2744">This can be contrasted with event-driven processing, in which the operating system alerts a program or routine to the occurrence of an event by means of an interrupt or message rather than having to check each device in turn.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2745">輪詢查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2745">polling query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2746">單一查詢，它會傳回值供 Analysis Services 用於判斷資料表或其他關聯式物件是否已變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2746">A singleton query that returns a value Analysis Services can use to determine if changes have been made to a table or other relational object.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2747">多邊形圖層 (polygon layer)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2747">polygon layer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2748">地圖報表中的圖層，會將空間資料顯示為國家/地區這類地理區域的圖層。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2748">The layer in a map report that displays spatial data as areas, for example, areas that indicate geographical regions such as counties.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2751">定點更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2751">positioned update</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2752">在資料列目前資料指標所在位置上執行的更新、插入或刪除作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2752">An update, insert, or delete operation performed on a row at the current position of the cursor.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2772">預先計算的資料分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2772">precomputed partition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2773">可用於篩選合併式發行集的效能最佳化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2773">A performance optimization that can be used with filtered merge publications.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2774">可預測資料行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2774">predictable column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2775">演算法會根據輸入資料行之值在周圍建立模型的資料採礦資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2775">A data mining column that the algorithm will build a model around based on values of the input columns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2776">除了做為輸出資料行之外，可預測資料行還可以做為相同採礦結構中，其他可預測資料行的輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2776">Besides serving as an output column, a predictable column can also be used as input for other predictable columns within the same mining structure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2777">prediction</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2777">prediction</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2778">資料採礦技術，它會分析現有的資料，再利用結果來預測新記錄的屬性值或現有記錄中遺漏屬性的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2778">A data mining technique that analyzes existing data and uses the results to predict values of attributes for new records or missing attributes in existing records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2779">例如，現有的信用應用程式資料可用於預測新應用程式的信用風險。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2779">For example, existing credit application data can be used to predict the credit risk for a new application.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2780">預測計算</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2780">Prediction Calculator</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2781">以羅吉斯迴歸分析為基礎的新報表，並且將每一個影響的因素與演算法計算出的分數一併呈現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2781">A new report that is based on logistic regression analysis and that presents each contributing factor together with a score calculated by the algorithm.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2782">此報表會以兩種形式呈現，一種是工作表，可幫助您輸入資料並計算可能的結果，另一種是書面報表，其功能與前者相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2782">The report is presented both as a worksheet that helps you enter data and make calculations of the probable outcomes, and as a printed report that does the same thing.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2783">前置詞字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2783">prefix characters</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2784">在原生格式大量複製資料檔中，在每個資料欄位前面的一組位元組 (1 至 4 位元組)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2784">A set of 1 to 4 bytes that prefix each data field in a native-format bulk-copy data file.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2789">展示模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2789">presentation model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2790">從資料存取層中的多個實體彙總資料的資料模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2790">A data model that aggregates data from multiple entities in the data access layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2791">用於避免對用戶端專案直接公開實體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2791">It is used to avoid directly exposing an entity to the client project.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2798">主索引鍵 (primary key)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2798">primary key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2799">唯一識別資料表中每一筆記錄的一個或多個欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2799">One or more fields that uniquely identify each record in a table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2800">與車牌號碼識別車輛的方式一樣，主索引鍵是記錄的唯一識別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2800">In the same way that a license plate number identifies a car, the primary key uniquely identifies a record.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2801">主要保護</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2801">primary protection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2802">在受保護伺服器上的保護類型，資料會直接受到主要 DPM 伺服器的保護。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2802">A type of protection in which data on the protected server is directly protected by a primary DPM Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2803">「主要資料庫」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2803">primary server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2804">在記錄傳送設定中，指主要資料庫所在的伺服器執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2804">In a log shipping configuration, the server instance where the primary database resides.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2805">主要資料表 (primary table)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2805">primary table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2806">在一對多關聯性中，兩份相關資料表的「一」這一端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2806">The "one" side of two related tables in a one-to-many relationship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2807">主要資料表應該有主索引鍵且每一筆記錄都應該是唯一的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2807">A primary table should have a primary key and each record should be unique.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2808">主體資料庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2808">principal database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2809">在資料庫採礦中，是指交易記錄會持續不斷傳送至鏡像伺服器的讀寫資料庫，該伺服器會將記錄還原到鏡像資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2809">In database mirroring, a read-write database whose transaction log is continuously sent to the mirror server, which restores the log to the mirror database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2810">主體伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2810">principal server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2811">資料庫鏡像中的夥伴，它的資料庫目前是主體資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2811">In database mirroring, the partner whose database is currently the principal database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2812">優先權提升</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2812">priority boost</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2813">一個進階選項，指定 Microsoft® SQL Server™ 是否應以高於同一部電腦上其他處理序的 Microsoft Windows NT® 排程優先權執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2813">An advanced option that specifies whether Microsoft® SQL Server™ should run at a higher Microsoft Windows NT® scheduling priority than other processes on the same computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2814">私密金鑰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2814">private key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2815">搭配公開金鑰演算法使用的密碼編譯金鑰組的密碼部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2815">The secret half of a cryptographic key pair that is used with a public key algorithm.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2816">一般來說，私密金鑰用來解密對稱工作階段金鑰、對資料進行數位簽署，或是針對使用對應公開金鑰加密的資料進行解密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2816">Private keys are typically used to decrypt a symmetric session key, digitally sign data, or decrypt data that has been encrypted with the corresponding public key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2817">主動式快取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2817">proactive caching</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2818">在 Cube 中管理資料陳舊過時的系統，其中 MOLAP 儲存體中的物件會在快取中自動更新和處理，而查詢會重新導向至 ROLAP 儲存體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2818">A system that manages data obsolescence in a cube by which objects in MOLAP storage are automatically updated and processed in cache while queries are redirected to ROLAP storage.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2819">程序快取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2819">procedure cache</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2820">在 SQL Server 記憶體集區中，用於儲存 Transact-SQL 批次、預存程序和觸發程序之執行計畫的部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2820">The part of the SQL Server memory pool that is used to store execution plans for Transact-SQL batches, stored procedures, and triggers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2821">設定檔範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2821">profile template</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2822">所有 Certificate Lifecycle Manager (CLM) 管理活動的核心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2822">The core of all Certificate Lifecycle Manager (CLM) management activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2823">設定檔範本會提供單一管理單位，其中包含管理多個憑證所需的所有資訊，而使用者群可能會在整個憑證生命週期中要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2823">The profile template provides a single administrative unit that includes all information necessary to manage the multiple certificates that might be required by a user community throughout the certificate's lifecycle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2824">設定檔範本還包括有關這些憑證之最終位置的資訊，可能是以軟體為基礎 (也就是儲存在本機電腦上)，或是以硬體為基礎 (儲存在智慧卡上)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2824">A profile template also includes information regarding the final location of those certificates, which can be software-based (that is, stored on the local computer) or hardware-based (stored on a smart card).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2825">設定檔範本無法同時包含軟體和智慧卡為基礎的憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2825">A profile template cannot include both software-based and smart card-based certificates.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2894">合格的元件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2894">qualified component</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2895">在 MSI 資料庫中直接藉由一對「元件類別目錄 GUID，字串限定詞」識別元件，而不是由元件識別項直接識別的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2895">A method of identifying a component in an MSI database indirectly by a pair "component category GUID, string qualifier" instead of identifying it directly by the component identifier.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2896">限定詞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2896">qualifier</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2897">包含描述類別、執行個體、屬性、方法或參數之資訊的修飾詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2897">A modifier containing information that describes a class, instance, property, method, or parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2898">限定詞是由通用資訊模型 (CIM)、CIM 物件管理員和開發人員所定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2898">Qualifiers are defined by the Common Information Model (CIM), by the CIM Object Manager, and by developers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2899">限定詞標註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2899">qualifier flavor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2900">旗標，提供有關限定詞的額外資訊，例如衍生類別或執行個體是否可以覆寫此限定詞的原始值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2900">A flag that provides additional information about a qualifier, such as whether a derived class or instance can override the qualifier's original value.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2901">配量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2901">quantum</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2902">特定執行緒在多工作業的作業系統中執行的一小段時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2902">A brief period of time when a given thread executes in a multitasking operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2903">它會先執行多工作業，然後才依據相同優先權的其他執行緒重新排程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2903">It performs the multitasking before it is rescheduled against other threads with the same priority.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2904">之前稱為「時間配量」(Time Slice)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2904">Previously known as a "time slice."</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2905">查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2905">query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2906">在 StreamInsight 伺服器中連續執行的查詢範本執行個體，這個伺服器會處理從查詢繫結之輸入配接器執行個體所收到的事件，並且將處理過的事件傳送至查詢所繫結的輸出配接器執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2906">An instance of a query template that runs continuously in the StreamInsight server processing events received from instances of input adapters to which the query is bound and sending processed events to instances of output adapters to which it is bound.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2907">查詢繫結器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2907">query binder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2908">將現有 StreamInsight 查詢範本繫結至特定輸入和輸出配接器的物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2908">An object that binds an existing StreamInsight query template to specific input and output adapters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2909">查詢繫結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2909">query binding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2910">將輸入配接器執行個體和輸出配接器執行個體繫結至查詢範本執行個體的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2910">The process of binding instances of input adapters and instances of output adapters to an instance of a query template.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2915">查詢提示</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2915">query hint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2916">指定所指出的提示應該用於整個查詢的提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2916">A hint that specifies that the indicated hints should be used throughout the query.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2917">查詢提示會影響陳述式中的所有運算子。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2917">Query hints affect all operators in the statement.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2918">查詢最佳化工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2918">query optimizer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2919">負責產生陳述式之有效執行計畫的資料庫引擎元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2919">A database engine component responsible for generating efficient execution plans for statements.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2931">RAD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2931">RAD</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2932">建置電腦系統的方法，其中系統會分區段進行程式撰寫和實作，而不是等到整個專案完成才實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2932">A method of building computer systems in which the system is programmed and implemented in segments, rather than waiting until the entire project is completed for implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2933">RAD 是由程式設計師 James Martin 所開發，會使用這類工具做為 CASE 和視覺化程式設計。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2933">Developed by programmer James Martin, RAD uses such tools as CASE and visual programming.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2934">不完全階層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2934">ragged hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2935">階層；在這個階層中，一個或多個階層分支的一個或多個層級並未包含成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2935">A hierarchy in which one or more levels do not contain members in one or more branches of the hierarchy.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2936">range</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2936">range</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2937">一組套用相同時鐘向量的連續項目識別碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2937">A set of continuous item identifiers to which the same clock vector applies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2938">範圍是以起點、結束點，以及套用至這兩點之間所有識別碼的時鐘向量來表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2938">A range is represented by a starting point, an ending point, and a clock vector that applies to all IDs that are in between.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2939">定界分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2939">range partition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2940">由特定且可自訂的資料範圍定義的資料表資料分割。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2940">A table partition that is defined by specific and customizable ranges of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2941">定界分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2941">range partitioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2942">資料表或索引的資料分割方式，它指定資料分割保存有單一分割資料行之值範圍的資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2942">A way of partitioning a table or index by specifying partitions to hold rows with ranges of values from a single partitioning column.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2950">變動率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2950">rate of change</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2951">相較於歷史資料的價格變動率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2951">The rate of price change compared with historical data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2952">變動率是依據目前價格之前的某個天數計算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2952">The rate of change is calculated against a period of days prior to the current price.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2953">輸出為百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2953">The output is a percentage.</span></span>|
