|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2974">記錄集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2974">record set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2975">由資料庫記錄群組所構成的資料結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2975">A data structure made up of a group of database records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2976">它的來源可以是基底資料表或資料表的查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2976">It can originate from a base table or from a query to the table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2977">recover</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2977">recover</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2978">指還原成穩定的狀況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2978">To put back into a stable condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2979">電腦使用者可能可以使用程式搜尋並搶救儲存體中留下的資訊，藉此復原遺失或損毀的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2979">A computer user may be able to recover lost or damaged data by using a program to search for and salvage whatever information remains in storage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2980">資料庫可以在某個問題造成損毀之後，藉由還原其完整性的方式復原，例如資料庫管理程式異常終止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2980">A database may be recovered by restoring its integrity after some problem has damaged it, such as abnormal termination of the database management program.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2981">recovery</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2981">recovery</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2982">使資料庫進入交易一致狀態的資料庫啟動階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2982">A phase of database startup that brings the database into a transaction-consistent state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2983">依據資料庫關閉的方式而定，復原可能包括向前復原記錄檔記錄中的所有交易 (重做階段)，以及回復未認可的交易 (恢復階段)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2983">Recovery can include rolling forward all the transactions in the log records (the redo phase) and rolling back uncommitted transactions (the undo phase), depending on how the database was shut down.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2984">復原分支</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2984">recovery branch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2985">共用相同復原分支 GUID 的 LSN 範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2985">A range of LSNs that share the same recovery branch GUID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2986">當資料庫建立時或 RESTORE WITH RECOVERY 產生復原分岔時，就會產生新的復原分支。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2986">A new recovery branch originates when a database is created or when RESTORE WITH RECOVERY generates a recovery fork.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2987">另外也可能是多分支復原路徑，其中包括涵蓋兩個或多個復原分岔點的 LSN 範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2987">A multiple-branch recovery path is possible that includes ranges of LSNs that cover two or more recovery fork points.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2988">復原分岔點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2988">recovery fork point</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2989">每次執行 RESTORE WITH RECOVERY 時，新復原分支開始的那一點 (LSN,GUID)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2989">The point (LSN,GUID) at which a new recovery branch is started, every time a RESTORE WITH RECOVERY is performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2990">每一個復原分岔決定復原分支之間的父子關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2990">Each recovery fork determines a parent-child relationship between the recovery branches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2991">如果您將資料庫復原到較早的時間點，並且從該時間點開始使用資料庫，則復原分岔點會開始新的復原路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2991">If you recover a database to an earlier point in time and begin using the database from that point, the recovery fork point starts a new recovery path.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2992">復原間隔</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2992">recovery interval</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2993">Database Engine 復原資料庫應該需要的最大時間量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2993">The maximum amount of time that the Database Engine should require to recover a database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2994">復原模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2994">recovery model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2995">用於控制資料庫備份和還原作業基本行為的資料庫屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2995">A database property that controls the basic behavior of backup and restore operations for a database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2996">例如，復原模式會控制交易的記錄方式、是否需要備份交易記錄，以及可用的還原作業種類。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2996">For instance, the recovery model controls how transactions are logged, whether the transaction log requires backing up, and what kinds of restore operations are available.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2997">復原路徑</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2997">recovery path</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2998">會使資料庫到達特定時間點 (稱為復原點) 的資料和記錄備份順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2998">The sequence of data and log backups that have brought a database to a particular point in time (known as a recovery point).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-2999">復原路徑是一組特定轉換，這些轉換會使資料庫隨時間而變化，同時又能維護資料庫的一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-2999">A recovery path is a specific set of transformations that have evolved the database over time, yet have maintained the consistency of the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3000">復原路徑描述從起點 (LSN,GUID) 到終點 (LSN,GUID) 的 LSN 範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3000">A recovery path describes a range of LSNs from a start point (LSN,GUID) to an end point (LSN,GUID).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3001">復原路徑中的 LSN 範圍從開始到結束可能會跨越一個或多個復原分支。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3001">The range of LSNs in a recovery path can traverse one or more recovery branches from start to end.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3002">復原點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3002">recovery point</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3003">在復原期間，向前復原作業在記錄鏈結中的停止點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3003">The point in the log chain at which rolling forward stops during a recovery.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3004">矩形 (rectangle)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3004">rectangle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3005">可當做多個報表項目之容器使用或在報表上當做圖形元素使用的報表項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3005">A report item that can be used as a container for multiple report items or as a graphical element on a report.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3006">遞迴階層 (recursive hierarchy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3006">recursive hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3007">這是會在資料中表示所有父子式關聯性的資料階層。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3007">A hierarchy of data in which all parent-child relationships are represented in the data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3008">遞迴資料分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3008">recursive partitioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3009">資料採礦演算法提供者使用的反覆程序，會將資料分組，直到找不到其他有用的群組為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3009">The iterative process, used by data mining algorithm providers, of dividing data into groups until no more useful groups can be found.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3010">重做</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3010">redo</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3011">復原期間的一個階段，它會將記錄的變更套用 (向前復原) 到資料庫，以採用較前面時段的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3011">The phase during recovery that applies (rolls forward) logged changes to a database to bring the data forward in time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3012">重做階段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3012">redo phase</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3013">復原期間的一個階段，它會將記錄的變更套用 (向前復原) 到資料庫，以採用較前面時段的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3013">The phase during recovery that applies (rolls forward) logged changes to a database to bring the data forward in time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3014">重做集合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3014">redo set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3015">要還原的所有檔案和頁面的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3015">The set of all files and pages being restored.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3016">參考資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3016">reference data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3017">依照共同的讀取作業和不頻繁的改變等特性分類的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3017">Data characterized by shared read operations and infrequent changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3018">參考資料的範例包括班機時刻表和產品目錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3018">Examples of reference data include flight schedules and product catalogs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3019">Windows Server AppFabric 提供了還原這類資料的本機快取功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3019">Windows Server AppFabric offers the local cache feature for storing this type of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3020">參考維度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3020">reference dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3021">維度與量值群組之間的關聯性，其中維度會透過另一個維度結合量值群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3021">A relationship between a dimension and a measure group in which the dimension is coupled to the measure group through another dimension.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3022">參考資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3022">reference table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3023">要在模糊查閱中使用的來源資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3023">The source table to use in fuzzy lookups.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3024">參考索引鍵</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3024">referenced key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3025">外部索引鍵所參考的主索引鍵或唯一索引鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3025">A primary key or unique key referenced by a foreign key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3026">參考索引鍵</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3026">referencing key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3027">資料庫資料表中的索引鍵，它來自於另一個資料表 (也稱為「參考資料表」) 而且它的值符合參考資料表中的主索引鍵 (PK) 或唯一索引鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3027">A key in a database table that comes from another table (also know as the "referenced table") and whose values match the primary key (PK) or unique key in the referenced table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3028">自反關聯性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3028">reflexive relationship</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3029">從資料表的某資料行或資料行組合到相同資料表其他資料行的關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3029">A relationship from a column or combination of columns in a table to other columns in that same table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3030">region</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3030">region</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3031">快取內的資料容器，它會將所有快取物件共同放置在單一快取主機上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3031">A container of data, within a cache, that co-locates all cached objects on a single cache host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3032">快取區域會藉由使用描述性字串 (稱為標記) 來啟用搜尋區域內所有快取物件的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3032">Cache Regions enable the ability to search all cached objects in the region by using descriptive strings, called tags.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3033">region</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3033">region</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3034">單一檔案中按照邏輯順序排列之 128 個分葉層級頁面的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3034">A collection of 128 leaf level pages in logical order in a single file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3035">可用於識別片段化的檔案區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3035">Used to identify areas of a file that are fragmented.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3036">註冊模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3036">registration model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3037">提交和核准註冊要求的既定方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3037">A defined method for submitting and approving enrollment requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3038">企業通常會選擇一種註冊模型，並且據此修改其管理原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3038">An enterprise generally chooses one registration model and modifies their management policies accordingly.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3039">迴歸</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3039">regression</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3040">根據資料集內的其他屬性，預測一個或多個連續變數的統計程序，例如利潤或損失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3040">The statistical process of predicting one or more continuous variables, such as profit or loss, based on other attributes in the dataset.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3041">迴歸輸入變數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3041">regressor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3042">輸入變數，其中包含與輸出變數的線性關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3042">An input variable that has a linear relationship with the output variable.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3043">關聯式資料庫管理系統 (relational database management system)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3043">relational database management system</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3044">資料庫系統，它會依照關聯式模型指定的方式，將資料組織成相關的資料列和資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3044">A database system that organizes data into related rows and columns as specified by a relational model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3045">關聯式引擎</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3045">relational engine</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3046">搭配儲存引擎運作的 SQL Server 元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3046">A component of SQL Server that works with the storage engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3047">它負責解譯 Transact-SQL 搜尋查詢，並找出最有效的方法，搜尋儲存引擎所提供未經處理的實體資料，最後將結果傳回給使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3047">It is responsible for interpreting Transact-SQL search queries and mapping out the most efficient methods of searching the raw physical data provided by the storage engine and returning the results to the user.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3048">關聯式 OLAP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3048">relational OLAP</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3049">利用關聯式資料庫中的資料表來儲存多維度結構的儲存模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3049">A storage mode that uses tables in a relational database to store multidimensional structures.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3050">關聯式存放區</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3050">relational store</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3051">資料儲存機制，它會根據關聯式模型結構化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3051">A data repository structured in accordance with the relational model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3052">關聯性物件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3052">relationship object</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3053">代表一對在彼此關聯性中扮演某個角色之物件的物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3053">An object representing a pair of objects that assume a role in relation to each other.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3054">相對日期</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3054">relative date</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3055">使用比較運算子所指定的日期範圍，可傳回某一日期範圍的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3055">A range of dates that is specified by using comparison operators and return data for a range of dates.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3056">遠端資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3056">remote data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3057">有別於 SQL Server 目前執行個體的 OLE DB 資料來源中所儲存的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3057">Data stored in an OLE DB data source that is separate from the current instance of SQL Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3058">遠端資料存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3058">remote data access</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3059">提供簡便方法的服務，讓智慧型裝置應用程式從遠端 SQL Server 資料庫資料表和本機 SQL Server Mobile Edition 資料庫資料表存取 (提取) 資料，並將資料傳送 (發送) 至這些資料庫資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3059">A service that provides a simple way for a smart device application to access (pull) and send (push) data to and from a remote SQL Server database table and a local SQL Server Mobile Edition database table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3060">RDA 也可以用來在執行 SQL Server 的伺服器上發出 SQL 命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3060">RDA can also be used to issue SQL commands on a server running SQL Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3061">遠端散發者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3061">remote Distributor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3062">設定成散發者的伺服器，且這個散發者有別於設定成發行者的伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3062">A server configured as a Distributor that is separate from the server configured as the Publisher.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3063">遠端登入識別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3063">remote login identification</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3064">指派給使用者的登入識別，以存取遠端伺服器上的遠端程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3064">The login identification assigned to a user for accessing remote procedures on a remote server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3065">遠端資料分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3065">remote partition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3066">資料儲存在執行 Analysis Services 執行個體之伺服器的資料分割，而不是用於儲存資料分割之中繼資料的資料分割。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3066">A partition whose data is stored on a server running an instance of Analysis Services, other than the one used to store the metadata of the partition.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3067">遠端服務繫結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3067">remote service binding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3068">指定遠端服務之本機安全性認證的 Service Broker 物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3068">A Service Broker object that specifies the local security credentials for a remote service.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3069">遠端預存程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3069">remote stored procedure</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3070">位於某個 SQL Server 執行個體上的預存程序，會由另外一個 SQL Server 執行個體上的陳述式執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3070">A stored procedure located on one instance of SQL Server that is executed by a statement on another instance of SQL Server.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3081">複本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3081">replica</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3082">位於 DPM 伺服器上單一磁碟區中，受保護資料的完整複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3082">A complete copy of protected data residing on a single volume on the DPM server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3083">每一個受保護的資料來源加入其保護群組之後，都會建立一個複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3083">A replica is created for each protected data source after it is added to its protection group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3084">在共置的情況下，多個資料來源的複本可以位於相同的複寫磁碟區上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3084">With co-location, multiple data sources can have their replicas residing on the same replica volume.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3085">複本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3085">replica</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3086">要進行同步處理之資訊的特定儲存機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3086">A particular repository of information to be synchronized.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3089">複寫機碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3089">replica key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3090">在複寫機碼對應中，對應至複寫識別碼的 4 位元組值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3090">A 4-byte value that maps to a replica ID in a replica key map.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3093">複寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3093">replication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3094">從某個位置 (一般是伺服器節點) 將內容和 (或) 組態設定複製到另一個位置的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3094">The process of copying content and/or configuration settings from one location, generally a server node, to another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3095">進行複寫可確保同步或容錯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3095">Replication is done to ensure synchronization or fault tolerance.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3098">報表產生器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3098">Report Builder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3099">一項報表撰寫工具，特色是具備類似 Microsoft Office 的撰寫環境以及多項其他功能，包括新的走勢圖、資料橫條及指標資料視覺化、能夠將報表項目儲存為報表組件、建立地圖的精靈、彙總各種彙總值，以及增強的運算式支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3099">A report authoring tool that features a Microsoft Office-like authoring environment and features such as new sparkline, data bar, and indicator data visualizations, the ability to save report items as report parts, a wizard for creating maps, aggregates of aggregates, and enhanced support for expressions.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3183">還原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3183">restore</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3184">一個多階段的程序，它會將指定之備份中的所有資料和記錄頁面複製到指定的資料庫中 (資料複製階段)，並且向前復原在備份中記錄的所有交易 (重做階段)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3184">A multi-phase process that copies all the data and log pages from a specified backup to a specified database (the data-copy phase) and rolls forward all the transactions that are logged in the backup (the redo phase).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3185">根據預設，此時還原會回復任何未完成的交易 (恢復階段)，這樣就會完成資料庫復原，並且供使用者使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3185">At this point, by default, a restore rolls back any incomplete transactions (the undo phase), which completes the recovery of the database and makes it available to users.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3186">還原順序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3186">restore sequence</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3187">一個或多個還原命令的順序，這些還原命令通常會初始化所要還原之資料庫、檔案和 (或) 頁面的內容 (資料複製階段)、向前復原所記錄的交易 (重做階段)，再回復未認可的交易 (恢復階段)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3187">A sequence of one or more restore commands that, typically, initializes the contents of the database, files, and/or pages being restored (the data-copy phase), rolls forward logged transactions (the redo phase), and rolls back uncommitted transactions (the undo phase).</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3223">回復</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3223">roll back</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3224">指反轉變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3224">To reverse changes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3225">向前復原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3225">roll forward</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3226">指將記錄的變更套用至向前復原集中的資料，使資料呈現較新的狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3226">To apply logged changes to the data in a roll forward set to bring the data forward in time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3227">向前復原集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3227">roll forward set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3228">依據還原順序還原的所有資料集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3228">The set of all data restored by a restore sequence.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3229">向前復原集是藉由還原一系列一個或多個資料備份所定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3229">A roll forward set is defined by restoring a series of one or more data backups.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3230">積存</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3230">roll up</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3231">從某一個位置中的多個位置收集資料的子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3231">To collect subsets of data from multiple locations in one location.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3319">次要保護</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3319">secondary protection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3320">保護類型，在受保護的伺服器上，資料會受到主要 DPM 伺服器保護，而主要 DPM 伺服器上的複本則受到次要 DPM 伺服器保護。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3320">A type of protection in which data on the protected server is protected by a primary DPM server and the replica on the primary DPM server is protected by a secondary DPM server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3321">「次要資料庫」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3321">secondary server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3322">在記錄傳送設定中，指的是次要資料庫所在的伺服器執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3322">In a log shipping configuration, the server instance where the secondary database resides.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3323">每隔一段時間，次要伺服器就會從主要資料庫複製最新的記錄備份，並且將記錄還原到次要資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3323">At regular intervals, the secondary server copies the latest log backup from the primary database and restores the log to the secondary database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3324">次要伺服器是暖待命伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3324">The secondary server is a warm standby server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3325">密碼提供者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3325">secret provider</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3326">一次密碼的產生和驗證元件，用於使用者驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3326">A one-time-password generation and validation component for user authentication.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3327">安全性實體 (securable)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3327">securable</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3328">可以利用權限來保護安全的實體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3328">Entities that can be secured with permissions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3329">最明顯的安全性實體為伺服器和資料庫，但是個別權限可以在更細微的層次進行設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3329">The most prominent securables are servers and databases, but discrete permissions can be set at a much finer level.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3330">安全通訊端層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3330">Secure Sockets Layer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3331">通訊協定，藉由使用資料加密、數位憑證和公開金鑰加密的組合提高資料通訊的安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3331">The protocol that improves the security of data communication by using a combination of data encryption, digital certificates, and public key cryptography.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3332">SSL 會啟用驗證並提升網路上的資料完整性與隱私權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3332">SSL enables authentication and increases data integrity and privacy over networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3333">SSL 不提供授權或不可否認性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3333">SSL does not provide authorization or nonrepudiation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3334">安全性延伸模組 (security extension)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3334">security extension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3335">在 Reporting Services 中，讓使用者或群組接受報表伺服器驗證的元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3335">A component in Reporting Services that authenticates a user or group to a report server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3336">安全性識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3336">security ID</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3337">在 Windows 系統中，用於識別企業內的使用者、群組或電腦帳戶的唯一值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3337">In Windows-based systems, a unique value that identifies a user, group, or computer account within an enterprise.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3338">每一個帳戶建立時，都會收到 SID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3338">Every account is issued a SID when it is created.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3339">安全性識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3339">security identifier</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3340">在 Windows 系統中，用於識別企業內的使用者、群組或電腦帳戶的唯一值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3340">In Windows-based systems, a unique value that identifies a user, group, or computer account within an enterprise.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3341">每一個帳戶建立時，都會收到 SID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3341">Every account is issued a SID when it is created.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3342">分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3342">segmentation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3343">資料採礦技術，它會分析資料來探索共用類似屬性集之記錄的互斥集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3343">A data mining technique that analyzes data to discover mutually exclusive collections of records that share similar attributes sets.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3344">自我聯結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3344">self-join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3345">在聯結欄位有相符的值時，將資料表中的記錄和相同資料表內的其他記錄結合起來的聯結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3345">A join in which records from a table are combined with other records from the same table when there are matching values in the joined fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3346">自我聯結可以是內部聯結或是外部聯結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3346">A self-join can be an inner join or an outer join.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3347">在資料庫圖表中，自我聯結稱為「自反關聯性」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3347">In database diagrams, a self-join is called a reflexive relationship.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3348">自助式註冊模型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3348">self-service registration model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3349">Certificate Lifecycle Manager (CLM) 註冊模型，其中憑證訂閱者會直接使用 Web 架構介面執行或要求憑證管理活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3349">A Certificate Lifecycle Manager (CLM) registration model in which a certificate subscriber performs or requests certificate management activities directly using a Web-based interface.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3370">序列化</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3370">serialization</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3371">將物件的狀態資訊轉換成可以存放或傳輸的表單之程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3371">The process of converting an object's state information into a form that can be stored or transported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3372">在序列化期間，物件將其目前的狀態寫入暫時或永久的儲存區，</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3372">During serialization, an object writes its current state to temporary or persistent storage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3373">之後可透過讀取或是還原序列化儲存區中的物件狀態，以重新建立該物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3373">Later, the object can be recreated by reading, or deserializing, the object's state from storage.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3399">工作階段 (session)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3399">session</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3400">連接為作用中且可進行通訊的一段時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3400">A period of time when a connection is active and communication can take place.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3401">基於在功能單元之間進行資料通訊的目的，工作階段也是指在建立、維護和釋放連接期間進行的所有活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3401">For the purpose of data communication between functional units, session also refers to all the activities that take place during the establishment, maintenance, and release of the connection.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3402">工作階段狀態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3402">session state</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3403">在 ASP.NET 中，針對目前使用者而建立在伺服器上的變數存放區；每一位使用者都會在伺服器上維護個別的工作階段狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3403">In ASP.NET, a variable store created on the server for the current user; each user maintains a separate Session state on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3404">工作階段狀態通常是用來儲存回傳之間的使用者特定資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3404">Session state is typically used to store user-specific information between postbacks.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3498">快照隔離等級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3498">snapshot isolation level</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3499">交易隔離等級，其中交易所執行的每個讀取作業都會傳回所有資料，就像交易一開始的資料一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3499">A transaction isolation level in which each read operation performed by a transaction returns all data as it existed at the start of the transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3500">由於快照集交易不會使用鎖定保護讀取作業，因此不會阻止其他交易修改快照集交易所讀取的任何資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3500">Because a snapshot transaction does not use locks to protect read operations, it will not block other transactions from modifying any data read by the snapshot transaction.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3501">快照式複寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3501">snapshot replication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3502">複寫，其中資料會精確地以其特定時點的形式散發，而且不會監視此資料的更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3502">A replication in which data is distributed exactly as it appears at a specific moment in time and does not monitor for updates to the data.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3557">疏鬆資料行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3557">sparse column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3558">資料行，會減少 Null 值的儲存需求，但要付出擷取非 Null 值的更多成本負擔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3558">A column that reduces the storage requirement for null values at the cost of more overhead to retrieve nonnull values.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3559">疏鬆檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3559">sparse file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3560">比其他方式需要更少磁碟空間進行處理的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3560">A file that is handled in a way that requires much less disk space than would otherwise be needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3561">疏鬆支援可讓應用程式建立非常大的檔案，卻不會因為檔案中只包含零的區域犧牲了磁碟空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3561">Sparse support allows an application to create very large files without committing disk space for those regions of the file that contain only zeros.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3562">例如，如果您只需要將前 64 KB 的資料寫入一個大小為 42 GB 的檔案，而其餘部分都是填入零，您就可以使用疏鬆支援處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3562">For example, you can use sparse support to work with a 42-GB file in which you need to write data only to the first 64 KB (the rest of the file is zeroed).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3563">稀疏性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3563">sparsity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3564">多維度結構未包含資料之資料格的相對百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3564">The relative percentage of a multidimensional structure's cells that do not contain data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3565">空間資料 (spatial data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3565">spatial data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3566">以 2D 或 3D 影像表示的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3566">Data that is represented by 2D or 3D images.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3567">空間資料可以進一步細分成幾何資料 (可以使用包含 Euclidian 幾何之計算的資料) 以及地理資料 (識別地球上地理位置和界限的資料)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3567">Spatial data can be further subdivided into geometric data (data that can use calculations involving Euclidian geometry) and geographic data (data that identifies geographic locations and boundaries on the earth).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3568">SPN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3568">SPN</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3569">用戶端用於唯一識別服務執行個體的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3569">The name by which a client uniquely identifies an instance of a service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3570">通常是從主機的 DNS 名稱建置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3570">It is usually built from the DNS name of the host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3571">SPN 是在用戶端與主控特定服務的伺服器之間相互驗證時所使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3571">The SPN is used in the process of mutual authentication between the client and the server hosting a particular service.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3655">SQL 追蹤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3655">SQL Trace</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3656">一組 Transact-SQL 系統預存程序，用來在 SQL Server Database Engine 的執行個體上建立追蹤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3656">A set Transact-SQL system stored procedures to create traces on an instance of the SQL Server Database Engine.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3663">SSAS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3663">SSAS</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3664">Microsoft SQL Server 的一項功能，可支援商業智慧應用程式的線上分析處理 (OLAP) 和資料採礦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3664">A feature of Microsoft SQL Server that supports online analytical processing (OLAP) and data mining for business intelligence applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3665">Analysis Services 會將資料倉儲中的資料組織成包含預先計算之彙總資料的 Cube，以便為複雜的分析查詢提供快速解答。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3665">Analysis Services organizes data from a data warehouse into cubes with precalculated aggregation data to provide rapid answers to complex analytical queries.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3666">SSL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3666">SSL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3667">通訊協定，藉由使用資料加密、數位憑證和公開金鑰加密的組合提高資料通訊的安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3667">The protocol that improves the security of data communication by using a combination of data encryption, digital certificates, and public key cryptography.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3668">SSL 會啟用驗證並提升網路上的資料完整性與隱私權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3668">SSL enables authentication and increases data integrity and privacy over networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3669">SSL 不提供授權或不可否認性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3669">SSL does not provide authorization or nonrepudiation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3670">SSRCT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3670">SSRCT</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3671">讓 DPM 管理員授權使用者執行自助式資料復原的工具，其方法是建立及管理 DPM 角色 (使用者、物件和權限的群組)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3671">A tool that enables DPM administrators to authorize end users to perform self-service recovery of data by creating and managing DPM roles (grouping of users, objects, and permissions).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3672">SSRS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3672">SSRS</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3673">伺服器架構的報表產生環境，適用於啟用 Web 的企業級報表功能，可讓您建立從各種資料來源取得內容的報表、以各種格式發行報表，以及集中管理安全性和訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3673">A server-based report generation environment for enterprise, Web-enabled reporting functionality so you can create reports that draw content from a variety of data sources, publish reports in various formats, and centrally manage security and subscriptions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3674">SSRT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3674">SSRT</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3675">使用者用來從 DPM 復原備份的工具，DPM 系統管理員不需要執行任何動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3675">A tool that is used by end users to recover backups from DPM, without any action required from the DPM administrator.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3676">暫存資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3676">staged data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3677">在 SQL Server Master Data Services 中的暫存處理序期間匯入至暫存資料表的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3677">Data imported into staging tables during the staging process in SQL Server Master Data Services.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3678">staging</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3678">staging</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3679">SQL Server Master Data Services 中用來將資料匯入至暫存資料表，然後將暫存資料當做批次進行處理，再匯入至 master 資料庫的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3679">The process used in SQL Server Master Data Services to import data into staging tables and then process the staged data as a batch prior to importing it into the master database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3680">暫存處理序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3680">staging process</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3681">SQL Server Master Data Services 中用來將資料匯入至暫存資料表，然後將暫存資料當做批次進行處理，再匯入至 master 資料庫的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3681">The process used in SQL Server Master Data Services to import data into staging tables and then process the staged data as a batch prior to importing it into the master database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3682">暫存佇列</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3682">staging queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3683">SQL Server Master Data Services 中的批次資料表，其中暫存記錄會當做批次佇列，以便之後處理至 Master Data Services 資料庫中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3683">The batch table in SQL Server Master Data Services where staged records are queued as batches to be processed into the Master Data Services database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3684">暫存資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3684">staging table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3685">SQL Server Master Data Services 中的資料表，其中會填入暫存處理序期間的商務資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3685">A table in SQL Server Master Data Services that is populated with business data during the staging process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3686">獨立伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3686">standalone server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3687">執行 Windows Server 但是未參與網域的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3687">A computer that runs Windows Server but does not participate in a domain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3688">獨立伺服器只有自己的使用者資料庫，而且會自行處理登入要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3688">A standalone server has only its own database of end users, and it processes logon requests by itself.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3689">它不會與其他電腦共用帳戶資訊，也無法提供網域帳戶的存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3689">It does not share account information with any other computer and cannot provide access to domain accounts.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3690">待命資料庫檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3690">standby file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3691">在還原作業的恢復階段期間，用於保存要修改的頁面之「寫入時複製」前置影像的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3691">In a restore operation, a file used during the undo phase to hold a "copy-on-write" pre-image of pages that are to be modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3692">待命資料庫檔案允許還原恢復階段，以回復未認可的交易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3692">The standby file allows reverting the undo pass to bring back the uncommitted transactions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3693">待命伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3693">standby server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3694">包含資料庫副本的伺服器執行個體，如果資料庫的來源副本無法使用，就可以將此資料庫副本上線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3694">A server instance containing a copy of a database that can be brought online if the source copy of the database becomes unavailable.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3695">記錄傳送可用於維護稱為次要伺服器的「暖」待命伺服器，這類伺服器的資料庫副本會定期從記錄備份自動更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3695">Log shipping can be used to maintain a "warm" standby server, called a secondary server, whose copy of the database is automatically updated from log backups at regular intervals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3696">在容錯移轉至暖待命伺服器之前，必須先手動讓其資料庫副本完全處於最新狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3696">Before failover to a warm standby server, its copy of the database must be brought fully up to date manually.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3697">資料庫鏡像可以用來維護稱為鏡像伺服器的「熱」待命伺服器，這類伺服器的資料庫副本會持續維持最新狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3697">Database mirroring can be used to maintain a "hot" standby server, called a mirror server, whose copy of the database is continuously brought up to date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3698">容錯移轉至鏡像伺服器上的資料庫實際上是在瞬間完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3698">Failover to the database on a mirror server is essentially instantaneous.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3699">常設查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3699">standing query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3700">在 StreamInsight 伺服器中執行之查詢範本的具現化，這個伺服器會針對內送事件執行連續運算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3700">An instantiation of a query template that runs within the StreamInsight server performing continuous computation over the incoming events.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3701">星型聯結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3701">star join</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3702">事實資料表 (通常是大型事實資料表) 和至少兩個維度資料表之間的聯結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3702">A join between a fact table (typically a large fact table) and at least two dimension tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3703">星型查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3703">star query</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3704">聯結一個事實資料表與一些維度資料表的查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3704">A query that joins a fact table and a number of dimension tables.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3705">星型結構描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3705">star schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3706">用在結構描述中心的單一事實資料表來維護資料的關聯式資料庫結構，其他維度資料儲存在維度資料表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3706">A relational database structure in which data is maintained in a single fact table at the center of the schema with additional dimension data stored in dimension tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3707">每個維度資料表都與事實資料表直接相關，且通常會藉由索引鍵資料行聯結到事實資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3707">Each dimension table is directly related to and usually joined to the fact table by a key column.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3708">開始角度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3708">start angle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3709">標尺開始旋轉的角度，介於 0 和 360 之間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3709">The angle of rotation, between 0 and 360, at which the scale will begin.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3710">零 (0) 的位置位於量測計底部，而且開始角度會順時針旋轉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3710">The zero (0) position is located at the bottom of the gauge, and the start angle rotates clockwise.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3711">例如，開始角度為 90 度時，標尺會在 9 點鐘的位置開始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3711">For example, a start angle of 90 degrees starts the scale at the 9 o'clock position.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3712">開始端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3712">start cap</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3713">線條的開頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3713">The start of a line.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3714">陳述式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3714">statement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3715">編譯的 T-SQL 查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3715">A compiled T-SQL query.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3716">靜態資料指標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3716">static cursor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3717">完全依照資料指標開啟時的狀態來顯示結果集的資料指標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3717">A cursor that shows the result set exactly as it was at the time the cursor was opened.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3718">靜態資料列篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3718">static row filter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3719">所有複寫類型都能使用的篩選，可讓您以 WHERE 子句為基礎來限制複寫到訂閱者的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3719">A filter available for all types of replication that allows you to restrict the data replicated to a Subscriber based on a WHERE clause.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3720">詞幹分析器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3720">stemmer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3721">在全文檢索搜尋中，字幹分析器會針對給定的語言，以這個語言的規則為基礎來產生特定單字的變化形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3721">In Full-Text Search, for a given language, a stemmer generates inflectional forms of a particular word based on the rules of that language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3722">字幹分析器為語言專用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3722">Stemmers are language specific.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3723">逐步執行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3723">step into</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3724">是指執行目前的陳述式並進入中斷模式，並且在達到另一個程序的呼叫時逐步執行下一個程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3724">To execute the current statement and enter Break mode, stepping into the next procedure whenever a call for another procedure is reached.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3725">監管中心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3725">stewardship portal</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3726">MDS 的一項功能，會透過包括成員和階層等主要資料提供集中控制，並且讓資料模型管理員透過開發、檢閱和管理資料模型並且跨網域一致強制執行的方式，確保資料的品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3726">A feature of MDS that provides centralized control over master data, including members and hierarchies and enables data model administrators to ensure data quality by developing, reviewing, and managing data models and enforcing them consistently across domains.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3727">庫存單位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3727">stock keeping unit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3728">產品的唯一識別碼，通常是英數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3728">A unique identifier, usually alphanumeric, for a product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3729">SKU 可針對存貨的目的用於追蹤產品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3729">The SKU allows a product to be tracked for inventory purposes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3730">SKU 可以與任何能夠購買的項目產生關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3730">An SKU can be associated with any item that can be purchased.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3731">例如，樣式編號 3726、尺寸 8 號的上衣，其 SKU 為 3726-8。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3731">For example, a shirt in style number 3726, size 8 might have a SKU of 3726-8.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3732">奪取分頁</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3732">stolen page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3733">緩衝區快取中針對其他伺服器要求所取得的頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3733">A page in Buffer Cache taken for other server requests</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3738">儲存引擎</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3738">storage engine</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3739">SQL Server 的元件，負責管理資料庫中未經處理的實體資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3739">A component of SQL Server that is responsible for managing the raw physical data in your database.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3740">例如，在磁碟中讀取和寫入資料是由儲存引擎所處理的工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3740">For example, reading and writing the data to disk is a task handled by the storage engine.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3746">預存程序解析程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3746">stored procedure resolver</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3747">程式，可叫用以處理資料列變更為主的衝突，這類衝突是在解析程式註冊所在的發行項中發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3747">A program that is invoked to handle row change-based conflicts that are encountered in an article to which the resolver was registered.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3748">資料流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3748">stream</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3749">位元組序列的抽象，例如，檔案、I/O 裝置、處理序間的通訊管道、TCP/IP 通訊端或多工緩衝處理列印工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3749">An abstraction of a sequence of bytes, such as a file, an I/O device, an inter-process communication pipe, a TCP/IP socket, or a spooled print job.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3750">複合檔案中資料流與儲存之間的關係，類似於檔案和資料夾之間的關係。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3750">The relationship between streams and storages in a compound file is similar to that of files and folders.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3814">SVG</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3814">SVG</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3815">二維圖形中與裝置無關之描述的 XML 架構語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3815">An XML-based language for device-independent description of two-dimensional graphics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3816">SVG 影像會在以不同畫面大小或解析度列印或檢視時維持其外觀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3816">SVG images maintain their appearance when printed or when viewed with different screen sizes and resolutions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3817">SVG 為全球資訊網協會 (World Wide Web Consortium，W3C) 所推薦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3817">SVG is a recommendation of the World Wide Web Consortium (W3C).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3818">掃掠角度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3818">sweep angle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3819">標尺將會在圓形中掃掠的度數，介於 0 和 360 之間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3819">The number of degrees, between 0 and 360 that the scale will sweep in a circle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3820">掃掠角度為 360 度時，會產生完整圓形的標尺。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3820">A sweep angle of 360 degrees produces a scale that is a complete circle.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3902">結尾記錄備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3902">tail-log backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3903">在可能損毀的資料庫上執行的記錄備份，以便擷取尚未備份的記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3903">A log backup taken from a possibly damaged database to capture the log that has not yet been backed up.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3904">結尾記錄備份是在發生失敗後進行，以防止遺失工作資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3904">A tail-log backup is taken after a failure in order to prevent work loss.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3987">交易記錄備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3987">transaction log backup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3988">交易記錄的備份，其中包括先前的記錄備份中所未備份的所有記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3988">A backup of transaction logs that includes all log records not backed up in previous log backups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3989">記錄備份為完整和大量記錄復原模式下所需，但無法在簡單復原模式下使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3989">Log backups are required under the full and bulk-logged recovery models and are unavailable under the simple recovery model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3990">交易保留週期</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3990">transaction retention period</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3991">在異動複寫中，交易儲存在散發資料庫中的時間量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3991">In transactional replication, the amount of time transactions are stored in the distribution database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3992">交易回復</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3992">transaction rollback</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3993">指將使用者指定的交易回復到交易內的上一個儲存點，或回復到交易的開頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3993">Rollback of a user-specified transaction to the last savepoint inside a transaction or to the beginning of a transaction.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3994">交易資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3994">transactional data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3995">與銷售量、出貨量、發票、問題票證、理賠，以及其他貨幣和非貨幣互動相關的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3995">Data related to sales, deliveries, invoices, trouble tickets, claims, and other monetary and non-monetary interactions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3996">異動複寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3996">transactional replication</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3997">通常開始於發行集資料庫物件和資料之快照集的複寫類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3997">A type of replication that typically starts with a snapshot of the publication database objects and data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3998">Transact-SQL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3998">Transact-SQL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-3999">包含用於管理 SQL Server 執行個體、建立和管理 SQL Server 執行個體中的所有物件，以及在 SQL Server 資料表中插入、擷取、修改和刪除所有資料之命令的語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-3999">The language containing the commands used to administer instances of SQL Server, create and manage all objects in an instance of SQL Server, and to insert, retrieve, modify and delete all data in SQL Server tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4000">Transact-SQL 是國際標準組織 (ISO) 和美國國家標準局 (ANSI) 發行的標準所定義之語言的延伸模組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4000">Transact-SQL is an extension of the language defined in the SQL standards published by the International Standards Organization (ISO) and the American National Standards Institute (ANSI).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4001">轉換</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4001">transformation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4002">修改、摘要說明和清理資料的 SSIS 資料流程元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4002">The SSIS data flow component that modifies, summarizes, and cleans data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4003">轉換輸入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4003">transformation input</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4004">這是包含在資料行中的資料，它會在聯結或查閱程序期間，用來修改或彙總它所聯結之資料表中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4004">Data that is contained in a column, which is used duing a join or lookup process, to modify or aggregate data in the table to which it is joined.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4005">轉換輸出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4005">transformation output</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4006">當做轉換程序之結果傳回的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4006">Data that is returned as a result of a transformation procedure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4007">趨勢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4007">Trend</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4008">普遍的傾向或趨向，通常是藉由檢查特定屬性一段時間的方式判斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4008">A general tendency or inclination, typically determined by the examination of a particular attribute over time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4009">信任連接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4009">trusted connection</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4010">Windows 網路連接，只能由經過網路驗證的使用者開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4010">A Windows network connection that can be opened only by users who have been authenticated by the network.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4013">輪轉視窗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4013">tumbling window</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4014">跳動大小等於視窗大小的跳動視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4014">A hopping window whose hop size is equal to the window size.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4015">Tuple</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4015">tuple</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4016">根據 Cube 中每個屬性階層之屬性成員的組合，唯一識別資料格的已排序成員集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4016">An ordered collection of members that uniquely identifies a cell, based on a combination of attribute members from every attribute hierarchy in the cube.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4017">兩階段認可</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4017">two-phase commit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4018">可確保多部伺服器所套用的交易，在所有伺服器中都能完成或都未完成的通訊協定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4018">A protocol that ensures that transactions that apply to more than one server are completed on all servers or none at all.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4019">兩階段認可是由交易管理員所協調，而且受到資源管理員所支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4019">Two-phase commit is coordinated by the transaction manager and supported by resource managers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4020">類型檢查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4020">type checking</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4021">由編譯器或解譯器所執行的處理序，可確保使用變數時，該變數會視為擁有宣告時所指的相同資料類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4021">The process performed by a compiler or interpreter to make sure that when a variable is used, it is treated as having the same data type as it was declared to have.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4022">具類型的配接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4022">typed adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4023">僅發出單一事件類型的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4023">An adapter that emits only a single event type.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4024">具類型的事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4024">typed event</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4025">已知來源所提供或接收所取用的事件裝載結構，而且輸入或輸出配接器設計於這個特定事件結構周圍的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4025">An event for which the structure of the event payload provided by the source or consumed by the sink is known, and the input or output adapter is designed around this specific event structure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4026">UCP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4026">UCP</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4027">網路節點，提供 SQL Server 公用程式的中央推理點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4027">A network node that provides the central reasoning point for the SQL Server Utility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4028">它使用 SQL Server Management Studio (SSMS) 中的公用程式總管組織及監視 SQL Server 資源健康情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4028">It uses Utility Explorer in SQL Server Management Studio (SSMS) to organize and monitor SQL Server resource health.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4029">UDT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4029">UDT</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4030">SQL Server 中純量類型系統的使用者撰寫延伸模組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4030">A user-written extension to the scalar type system in SQL Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4031">不對稱階層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4031">unbalanced hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4032">階層；在這個階層中，一個或多個階層分支的一個或多個層級並未包含成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4032">A hierarchy in which one or more levels do not contain members in one or more branches of the hierarchy.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4033">未繫結資料流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4033">unbound stream</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4034">包含事件模型或裝載類型之定義，但沒有定義資料來源的事件資料流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4034">An event stream that contains the definition of the event model or payload type, but does not define the data source.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4035">無法認可</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4035">uncommittable</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4036">與維持開啟而且無法完成的交易相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4036">Pertaining to a transaction that remains open and cannot be completed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4037">無法認可的交易可視為部分失敗交易的子類別，其中交易發生錯誤而無法完成，但是仍然保留其鎖定而且須由使用者回復。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4037">Uncommitable transactions could be considered a subclass of partially failed transactions, where the transaction has encountered an error that prevents its completion, but it is still holding its locks and has to be rolled back by the user.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4038">解壓縮</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4038">uncompress</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4039">是指將壓縮檔的內容還原成其原始形式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4039">To restore the contents of a compressed file to its original form.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4040">無法傳遞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4040">undeliverable</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4041">無法傳遞至預期的收件者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4041">Not able to be delivered to an intended recipient.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4042">如果電子郵件無法傳遞，就會傳回至寄件者，其中包含郵件伺服器加入之說明問題的資訊，例如電子郵件地址可能不正確，或是收件者的信箱已滿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4042">If an e-mail message is undeliverable, it is returned to the sender with information added by the mail server explaining the problem; for example, the e-mail address may be incorrect, or the recipient's mailbox may be full.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4043">基礎資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4043">underlying table</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4044">檢視表、資料指標或預存程序所參考的資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4044">A table referenced by a view, cursor, or stored procedure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4045">恢復</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4045">undo</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4046">資料庫復原期間的一個階段，它會反轉 (回復) 在復原的重做階段完成時尚未認可之任何交易所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4046">The phase during database recovery that reverses (rolls back) changes made by any transactions that were uncommitted when the redo phase of recovery completed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4047">恢復檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4047">undo file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4048">一個檔案，它會在未認可的回復交易修改過資料庫中的頁面內容之後，以及復原將頁面內容還原至先前狀態之前，儲存該頁面內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4048">A file that saves the content of the pages in a database after they've been modified by uncommitted, rolled back transactions and before recovery restores them to their previous state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4049">恢復檔案可避免未認可交易所執行的變更遺失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4049">The undo file prevents the changes performed by uncommitted transactions from being lost.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4050">恢復階段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4050">undo phase</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4051">資料庫復原期間的一個階段，它會反轉 (回復) 在復原的重做階段完成時尚未認可之任何交易所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4051">The phase during database recovery that reverses (rolls back) changes made by any transactions that were uncommitted when the redo phase of recovery completed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4052">非強制關聯性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4052">unenforced relationship</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4053">資料表之間的一項連結，它將一份資料表中的主索引鍵關聯到另一份資料表中的外部索引鍵，但在 INSERT 和 UPDATE 交易期間，不會檢查參考完整性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4053">A link between tables that references the primary key in one table to a foreign key in another table, and which does not check the referential integrity during INSERT and UPDATE transactions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4054">未初始化</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4054">uninitialize</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4055">是指變更列舉值或資料來源物件的狀態，使其無法用來存取資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4055">To change the state of an enumerator or data source object so that it cannot be used to access data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4056">唯一索引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4056">unique index</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4057">不允許任兩個資料列有相同索引值的索引，因而會禁止重複的索引或索引鍵值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4057">An index in which no two rows are permitted to have the same index value, thus prohibiting duplicate index or key values.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4058">唯一識別值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4058">uniqueifier</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4059">一個 4 位元組資料行，SQL Server Database Engine 會自動將它加入資料列中，使每個索引鍵成為唯一的索引鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4059">A 4-byte column that the SQL Server Database Engine automatically adds to a row to make each index key unique.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4060">世界標準時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4060">Universal Time Coordinate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4061">世界各地皆通用的標準時間，由國際度量衡局 (International Bureau of Weights and Measures) 協調。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4061">The standard time common to every place in the world, coordinated by the International Bureau of Weights and Measures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4062">世界標準時間用於同步處理網際網路上的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4062">Coordinated Universal Time is used for the synchronization of computers on the Internet.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4063">未知的成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4063">unknown member</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4064">在處理包含維度的 Cube 期間，找不到任何索引鍵之維度的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4064">A member of a dimension for which no key is found during processing of a cube that contains the dimension.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4065">未知的磁帶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4065">unknown tape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4066">DPM 伺服器尚未識別的磁帶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4066">Tape that has not been identified by the DPM server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4067">Unmanaged 程式碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4067">unmanaged code</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4068">在 .NET Framework Common Language Runtime 外部，直接由作業系統執行的程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4068">Code that is executed directly by the operating system, outside the .NET Framework common language runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4069">Unmanaged 程式碼必須提供自己的記憶體管理、型別檢查和安全性支援，不像 Managed 程式碼會從 Common Language Runtime 接收這些服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4069">Unmanaged code must provide its own memory management, type checking, and security support, unlike managed code, which receives these services from the common language runtime.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4070">未受管理的執行個體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4070">unmanaged instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4071">未受公用程式控制點監視的 SQL Server 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4071">An instance of SQL Server not monitored by a utility control point.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4072">取消樞紐</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4072">unpivot</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4073">是指將單一記錄中多個資料行的值擴充為單一資料行中具有同一值的多個記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4073">To expand values from multiple columns in a single record into multiple records with the same values in a single column.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4074">不安全的程式碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4074">unsafe code</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4075">在 .NET Framework Common Language Runtime 外部，直接由作業系統執行的程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4075">Code that is executed directly by the operating system, outside the .NET Framework common language runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4076">Unmanaged 程式碼必須提供自己的記憶體管理、型別檢查和安全性支援，不像 Managed 程式碼會從 Common Language Runtime 接收這些服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4076">Unmanaged code must provide its own memory management, type checking, and security support, unlike managed code, which receives these services from the common language runtime.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4077">不具類型的配接器 (untyped adapter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4077">untyped adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4078">接受或發出多種事件類型的配接器，而且事先不知道裝載結構或裝載中的欄位類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4078">An adapter that accepts or emits multiple event types in which the payload structure or the type of fields in the payload are not known in advance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4079">範例包括 CSV 或文字檔、SQL 資料表或通訊端中的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4079">Examples are events from a CSV or text file, a SQL table, or a socket.</span></span>|
