|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4109">version</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4109">version</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4110">用於區別快取中使用相同索引鍵儲存之物件的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4110">A property that is used to differentiate objects stored in the cache using the same key.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4111">Windows Server AppFabric 會使用 DataCacheItemVersion 類別儲存版本資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4111">Windows Server AppFabric stores the version information using the DataCacheItemVersion class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4112">每次快取中加入物件或物件更新，版本值就會改變。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4112">Every time an object is added or updated in the cache, the version value changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4113">版本設定用於維護資料的一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4113">Versioning is used to maintain data consistency.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4114">開放式並行就是藉由使用相對於鎖定的版本設定達成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4114">Optimistic concurrency is achieved by using versioning as opposed to locks.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4115">version</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4115">version</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4116">識別對複本中某個項目所進行變更的中繼資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4116">Metadata that identifies a change made to an item in a replica.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4117">其中包含該項目的複寫機碼及複寫滴答計數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4117">It consists of the replica key and the replica tick count for the item.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4118">垂直篩選 (vertical filtering)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4118">vertical filtering</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4119">篩選資料表中的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4119">Filtering columns from a table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4120">在複寫中使用它時，所建立的資料表發行項只會包含發行資料表中選取的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4120">When used as part of replication, the table article created contains only selected columns from the publishing table.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4121">垂直資料分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4121">vertical partitioning</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4122">是指根據選取的資料行，將單一資料表分割成多個資料表的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4122">The process of splitting a single table into multiple tables based on selected columns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4123">這些資料表中，每一個都包含相同數目的資料列，但是包含較少的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4123">Each of the multiple tables has the same number of rows but fewer columns.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4124">垂直分割</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4124">vertical split</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4125">CIDER 介面的垂直方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4125">A vertical orientation of the CIDER shell.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4126">大型資料庫 (very large database)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4126">very large database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4127">這是已經變得很大而足以成為管理挑戰的資料庫，需要人員額外注意和處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4127">A database that has become large enough to be a management challenge, requiring extra attention to people, processes, and processes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4128">犧牲者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4128">victim</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4129">當 tempdb 用盡空間而 Database Engine 強制縮小版本存放區時，執行最久且未產生資料列版本的交易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4129">The longest running transaction that has not generated row versions when tempdb runs out of space and the Database Engine forces the version stores to shrink.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4130">在錯誤記錄檔中會針對每一筆犧牲者交易產生訊息 3967。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4130">A message 3967 is generated in the error log for each victim transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4131">如果交易已標示為犧牲者，它就不能再讀取版本存放區中的資料列版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4131">If a transaction is marked as a victim, it can no longer read the row versions in the version store.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4148">暖待命</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4148">warm standby</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4149">備援方法，其中次要 (也就是備份) 系統會在主要系統的背景中執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4149">A method of redundancy in which the secondary (i.e., backup) system runs in the background of the primary system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8e4be-4150">資料會定期鏡像至次要伺服器，這表示兩部伺服器會有未包含完全相同資料的時候。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e4be-4150">Data is mirrored to the secondary server at regular intervals, which means that there are times when both servers do not contain the exact same data.</span></span>|
